1a1(rgyud 'grel): rdo rje sems dpa' sgyu 'phrul dra ba le'u stong phrag brgya pa las rtsa ba'i rgyud dpal gsang ba snying po'i don bsdus 'brel pid+d+hAn+da bzhugs so// lca gar kyi baN+Di t+ta chen po bI ma la mi tras mdzad pa'o//
1b1(rgyud 'grel): maldan 'das dpa 'gan tu mang
1b2(rgyud 'grel): phyag 'tshal lo// mnyam nyid dbyis su bdud
2a1(rgyud 'grel): #bzhi ngang gis bcom// phyag rgya'i rang bzhin gnyis med rdzogs par ldan// yo med mtha' 'das bdag
2a2(rgyud 'grel): gzhan yongs kyi dpal// thams cad rang bzhin rtogs dang thugs rje bzang // kun bzang lha'i lha khyod dbyer med la// rtogs
2a3(rgyud 'grel): dang grub pas rab tu phyag 'tshal lo// gang zhig sgyu 'phrul dra ba'i rgyud 'di nyid// don rtogs gsal bar bya phyir bdag gis
2b1(rgyud 'grel): ni don bsdus rab tu dbye ba 'di brtsam pas// dngos grub mchog gnyis thob par bya phyir bshad// gang gis rgyud 'di rtogs dka' bas// bde rlag du ni rtogs par 'gyur
2b2(rgyud 'grel): di yi rang bzhin che ba dang // mtshan nyid dang ni don bstan phyir// sgyu 'phral dra ba'i rgyud chen las// mdor bsdus bstan la phab pa yin// rang bzhin gsang ba zhes pa ste// che ba
2b3(rgyud 'grel): rdo snying po'i don// de kho na nyid mtshan nyid// nges pas nges don mdor bstan pa// de ltar rnam pa bzhi po ru// mdor bsdus spyi'i don du bshad// rang bzhin gab dang rdos pa dang //
2b4(rgyud 'grel): stan min zhes bya'i rang bzhi ni// mnyam pa nyid dang dgongs pa'i don// mdzad spyod gsang ba'i theg pa nyid// rnam bzhi gsang ba zhes pa'i mtshan// sde snod rgyud kun 'byung phyir dang // bstan
3a1(rgyud 'grel): la 'debs dang khyad par che// ston pa 'khor dang gnas las sogs// mchog tu gyur pas che ba bshad// rgyu dang 'bras bu dbyer med pa// don dam kun rdzob gnyis med ni// mtshan nyid zhes bya ba rnam pa gsum// lung
3a2(rgyud 'grel): dang man ngag nges pa yang // nges pa'i dbyings nas byung bas na// nges don don ni bstan pa yin// nges don spyi'o mtshan nyid ni// so so rnam grangs don rnams kyi// sngon du 'gro ba'i bdag nyid pas// ming ni nyid thog mar smos pa gces// rgyu dang rkyen dang
3a3(rgyud 'grel): nga nyid dang // 'gro ba'i don du snang ba'i phyir// gleng gzhi dang ni gleng spangs te// don dang yongs su gzung ba dang // rnam pa bzhi ni bsdus pa yin// gleng gzhi rnam pa lngar bshang nge// gang tshe gang gi gang du bshad// gang la gang gis bsdus pa ste// 'byung ba
3a4(rgyud 'grel): sa dang ston pa dang // gnas dang 'khor dang sdud pa'o// sgo dang skur ba zhi bas na// 'di skad zhes su bshad pa yin// sku gsung thugs kyis bshad pas na// ma rtogs ston dang gsung thos ston// bshad ces pas ni spangs pa yin// bla med 'khor lo bskor
3a5(rgyud 'grel): de tshe dus zhes bya bar grags// ston pa zhes pa'i mtshan nyid ni// rang bzhin dang ni mdzad spyod dang // rnal 'bo rnam gnyis ngo la snang // byang chub chen po'i rang bzhin dang // chos rnams rol par longs spong dang // phyogs dus bde gshegs
3a6(rgyud 'grel): bdag po dang // chos so tsog dang dbyer med pa// ston pa'i rang bzhin rnam pa bzhi// don dam chos kyi sku'i mtshan// mdzad spring gzugs sku rnam gnyis te// longs spyong rdzogs dang sprul sku'o// longs spyong sngags kyi bdag po'i tshul// rgyal po rgyal mo yang
3b1(rgyud 'grel): yang dag ldan// sprul pa rdul snyed thub pa dang // khro rgyal stsogs pa grangs med yin// bdag po sku'i mtshan nyid dang // zhal dang mtshan dang dpe byad dang // bsam 'das zhabs dang phyag mtshan dang // dbu dang sku dang / kha dog dang // rgyal mo'i tshogs
3b2(rgyud 'grel): dang bzhugs pa'i dpe// bcu dang gsum gyis rdzogs par rol// ye shes phyi nang med pa dang // thams cad mnyam par dgongs pa dang // semos dpa' sems mar ldan pa dang // bcu drug rgyas btab dpe byad dang // lus dang ngag sems cis 'dus par
3b3(rgyud 'grel): dede de da / sku gsung snang ba dang // thabs dang shes rab snang ba dang // ye shes drug dang phyag rgya drug/ rnam thar sku gsung bsam yas dang // phung po lnga po'i ngo bo nyid// rgyal ba lnga ru rdzogs sangs rgyas// kun kyang kha dog lnga pa ste// nyi shu rtsa lnga rin
3b4(rgyud 'grel): mdog/ snang bar mnyen dro bskyod dang lnga// dbyings kyi ngo bo rgyal mo ste// de bzhin kr-i te rnam lnga min// na mkha' dbyings kyi mtha' klas pa// ston pa'i mdzad spyod rol mo yis// til gyi gang bu bzhin du khyab// ston pa 'i khang bar yin par grags//
3b5(rgyud 'grel): gnas ni rnam pa gsum du grags// chos kyi dbyings dang gzhal yas khang // ba kha chos 'byung zhes su bya// mtha' dbus med pa chos kyi dbyings// de ni gnas kyi bla mar 'dod// gzhal yas bzhi dang rgyu dang rgya// dbyibs dang blo 'bur rtse mo dang //
3b6(rgyud 'grel): rgyan dang sgo khyud rta babs dang // mtshan nyid gdon gyi rnam pa ste// bcu gcig dag gis rnam par dbye'o// gzhi'i yang tshad med 'khor lo ste// ye shes lnga yi rang bzhin yin// ye shes phyogs bzhi dbus brtags pas// rin chen las byas
4a1(rgyud 'grel): gzhal yas khang // che chung yo bu ma byas pa// chos dbyings mtha' la khyab par snang // rgyas par rgyas phyir gru bzhi pa'o// kun las spags pa'i gzungs bzhi dang // ye shes pa'o'i ngo bo nyid// gcog la'ang ye shes kun gnas dang /
4a2(rgyud 'grel): gzhal bas mdzes par byas pa'i phyir// glo 'bur bzhi yang mkhar thabs tshul// bum pa'i rtse mo chos kyi rtog/ chos kyi dbyings su kun nas gnas// glo 'bur lnga'i brgyan rnams kyang // dbyibs dang kha dog bye brag dag/ rigs kyi khyad par gyis ni dbye
4a3(rgyud 'grel): gnas mchog nyid kyi rgya ni mchog kyang // gzugs sgra dri ro reg gi rnams// rigs kyi khyang par gyis ni brtag/ so sor ma bsgrib ngang gis gsal// bar chad med par phyogs bcur 'khrigs// stong smon mtshan med 'od gsal 'jug/ de phyir ye shes
4a4(rgyud 'grel): sgo khrung can// nyan thos rang rgyal byang chub dang // bya ba rgyud dang gnyis gu rgyud// rnal 'byor skyed dang rdzogs pa yi// rnam thar brgyad phyir rta babs brgyad// gnas mchog mtshan nyid brjod pa ni// gzhal yas phyi dang chos dbyings nang // bdag nyid du bsdus bas na
4a5(rgyud 'grel): kun du nang zhes bshad pa yin// do na gnas pa'i god na mchog kyang // sang+ge gling chen rta dang khyung // nam mkha' lding gi khri chen la// nyi zla pad+ma rin po che// lnga rdzogs nyi shu rtsa lngar ldan// rgyal po rgyal mo'i gdan mchog la// mi 'jigs bzhi dang stobs bcu dang // rdzu 'phrul
4a6(rgyud 'grel): ba'i ngang dbang rnams bcu// logs med 'brim pas rnam pa'i'o// babs dang shes rab 'ong gsal 'bar// skyon gyis mgos pang ma shes// sngon sangs rgyas dang bag pa'ang // bar mchod dang nges par 'byung // 'jig rten 'jig rten 'das bcas la// 'jigs
4b1(rgyud 'grel): med pa'i sems kyis su// chos kyi 'khor lo rab tu bskor// gnas dang gnas min yang dag ma khyen// dus gsum las 'das rnam smin mkhyen// khams rnams sna tshogs mkhyen pa dang // pha rol mos pa mkhyen pa'i stobs// dbang po mchog dang
4b2(rgyud 'grel): mchog min mkhyen// kun du 'gro lam mkhyen pa'i'o stobs// bsam gtan par dang nyon mongs mkhyen// sngon gyi gnas mkhyen stobs dang ni// skye dang 'chi 'pho mkhyen pa dang // zag pA zag med sems grol mkhyen// de bcu stobs bcur gyur pas na//
4b3(rgyud 'grel): 'bras bu sngon shes drug yin no// 'dun dang brtson 'grus sems dang nI// spyod pa'i ting 'dzin spong ba yini// 'du byed rnams te rkang pa bzhi// ye shes bani grub 'bros bu ste// chos dbyings ye shes kun la khyab// yo byad skye bo che la dbang // ye shes chos pa
4b4(rgyud 'grel): sems dang las// rdzu 'phrul smon lam mos rnams kyi// khams kun gyis ni dbang phyug rgyal// zhi rgyas dbang dug las rnams kyis// thog med las rnams lhun gyis grub// ci la thogs pa med par spyod// gnas mchog khyad par de nyid kyang // dbyings
4b5(rgyud 'grel): byug pa gar bstan pa yin// 'khor rnams bkod pa ji snyed pa// khams dang skye mched yin par grags// rnam shes yul dang dbang po dang // dus dang phyin ci ma log rnams// byang chub chen po'i rang bzhin du// lhun gyis grub pa'i dkyil 'khor yin// mthong
4b6(rgyud 'grel): dang thos dang snoms dang myong // rnam shes bzhi po sems dpar shar// mthong bya thos bya snoms bya dang // myong bya 'dod pa'i lha mo rnams// rnam shes bzhi dang dbyer med par// mdzes de'i glo 'bur bzhi po la// nyi zla pad+ma rin chen gang na// mthong byed thos byed snoms
5a1(rgyud 'grel): khyed dang // myong byed dbang po'i sems dpa' dang // 'das dang dA lngar byung bong dang // 'byung bar ma nges lha mo bzhi// dbyer med tshul du grwa ba'i gnas// reg pa reg byed reg bya dang // yid kyi khams te 'joms byed dang // rtag chang bdag tu ma yin dang / ma
5a2(rgyud 'grel): ma ma yin 'joms pa rnams// sgo bzhi pogs su de bzhin gnas// kun bzang yid kyi rnam shes dang // chos ni bya ba kun du bzang // mdun dang rgyab du rnam par gnas// de nyid bsdud pa phun sum tshogs// bsdu bya'i yul ni chos yin te// byed pa po ni kun tu bzang // thugs kyi
5a3(rgyud 'grel): thugs te thugs yin no// srid gsum 'gro ba thams cad kyis// phung po khams dang skye mched dag/ brjod med brjod kyis mi langs pa// de snyed 'khor lo dkyil 'khor du// sngon rdzogs rgyal po de nyid nges// gnyis med lhun grub dkyil 'khor na// thams cad bdag nyid
5a4(rgyud 'grel): rtag tu bzhugs// de nas ston pa bang gshegs rnams// btsun mo'i tshigs dang gnyis med pa'i// gsang ba mchog gi dkyil 'khor rnams// rgyud 'di nyid kyi mdo don ste// dkyil 'khor kun gyi gsang ba 'di// sku gsung yin tan 'phrin las thugs// rdo rje las ni nges
5a5(rgyud 'grel): ra byung // ngo mtshar dkyil 'khor brjod pa'i tshig/ e zhes bya ba dam pa'i don// e ma zhes bya rab tu ngam// e ma ho zhes bya shin tu ngam// dkyil 'khor rnam pa bcu gnyis te// de bzhin nyid dang rang bzhin dang // thugs rjes 'dul ba'i dkyil 'khor dang // ting nge 'dzin
5a6(rgyud 'grel): dang gzugs brnyan dang // lhag pa'i ting 'dzin gzugs brnya no dang // byang chub sems dang lhag bang sems// tshegs dang lhun grub dkyil 'khor ro// chos kyi dbyings nyid de bzhin nyid// ye shes kyis ni dbang sgyur ba// rang bzhin thabs kyis dkyil 'khor nyid// thug
5b1(rgyud 'grel): byung ba thugs rje'o// de nyid thugs rjes 'dul ba'i ngang // rang snang dbyer med dkyil 'khor du// ting nge 'dzin gyis rnam par bsgom// rten 'byung mtshon par byed pas na// gzugs brnyan sgyu ma'i dkyil 'khor ni// sgyu ma yin zhes rgyal bas gsungs// mkha' dbyings
5b2(rgyud 'grel): gsal bar rnams spyad pas// de yang rang snang zhes su bshad// sku gsung yon tan 'phrin las thugs// de nyid mtshon pa'i thabs tshul du// sa la sogs la phyag rgya byas// lhag pa'i gzugs brnyan yin par grags// dam pa'i don gyi byang chub sems// til 'bru
5b3(rgyud 'grel): bzhin ni kun la khyab// a'i po de rab tu bsdus// byang chub rdo rje dri las byung // lhag pa yid bzhin rin po che// sku gsung thugs ni mi zad pa// gter ldan brgyan gyi 'khor lo nyid// tshogs chen rdzogs bces su bshad// chos sku rdo rje mchog nyid ngo // ma bcos lhun grub
5b4(rgyud 'grel): bdag nyid do// mnyam nyid dbyings kyi ngo bzhin nyid// man zhes bya ba snying po'i don// da la zhes bya len pa'o// yul dang dbang po yin par dgongs// spyod yul kun du maN+Da la// rdo rje gsang bas gsung ba dang // brjod dka' de nyid brjod pas na// rdo rje gsang po'i tshig du'o//
5b5(rgyud 'grel): brjod du med pabri ngo bo nyid// tshig du brjod pa ma yin+da yang // 'dzub mo sgron ma zla ba gser// don mtshon tshig ni don dang 'dra// don ni mi rtogs med mon pa'o// dbul baM'i gter dang gyang nor 'dra// tshig ni me long sgron ma'i tshul// 'gro ba'i don la brjod par bshad//
5b6(rgyud 'grel): des na bde gshegs rgyal ba rnams// nyid la nyid kyis gsung mod kyi// 'gro la phan pa'i don gyi phyir// brjod pa nyid du rgyal bas gsung // gleng bzhi'i le'u ste dang po'o// di nas ston pa rgyal mchog gis// dkyil 'khor mdo don gleng ba// de nyid don
6a1(rgyud 'grel): dzang bsdus 'dod nas// sang yum gnas po gleng ba yin// ya k+Sha sa gas da rmongs pa// gangagis pa lta gang glengs dang // grangs pa'i 'bras bu nyid dang can// thams cad kun gyi byed pa 'o// kun pazang ying rnying rdu te// ye shes rdo rje 'dus pa
6a2(rgyud 'grel): tshul/ rang rig dbyings la 'jug 'gyur te// srid dang rnam grol thams cad kun// thig le'i tshul du dbyer med pas// ston pa rdo rje bde gshegs la// kun ba'ang bde bar gshegs nyid kyis// 'gro ba'i mching du 'di skad brjod// rang gi 'khor lo'i dkyil 'khor la/
6a3(rgyud 'grel): mtshar gyis ni tshig brjod de// srid dang rnam grol thams cad kyi// phung po'i yan lag rnam pa lnga// chos sku rdo rje yin pa'i phyir// rgyal po lnga ru rnam par grags// 'gro ba'i 'gro ba thams cad kyi// khams dang skye mched rnam pa kun// sems pa sems ma'i dkyil 'khor
6a4(rgyud 'grel): yin pa khams lnga dbyings phyag rgyal mo lnga// mdor na snying gsum thams cad kun// mngon rdzogs rgyal por de nyid nges// 'di skad tshig du gleng ba'i tshe// rgyal ba rigs lnga'i dkyil 'khor rnams// 'gro ba'i ched du mnyes gyur nas// yum gyi dbyings kyi don glengs pa// gang
6a5(rgyud 'grel): gis ji ltar/ ji skad glengs// glengs pa'i 'bras bu nyid dang bzhi// bya ba mo ni kun du bzang // ye shes la ni dbyings phyug 'gyur// 'gro ba'i ched du gleng ba ni// stong gsum rdul snying phyogs bcu kun// dngos por ma grub ye nas dbyen// srid gsum 'gro ba'i gnas nyid la/
6a6(rgyud 'grel): zhing khams dag las gud na med// nyon mongs dus tshe lta ba sems can nyid// snyigs ma lnga po 'gro ba'i sdug bsngal te// bde chen gnas nyid las ni gzhan ma yin// nye bar len pa'i phung po lnga po las// bde gshegs gud na yod ma yin// de bas thams cad
6b1(rgyud 'grel): snying po'i mchog/ gzhan du sangs rgyas rtsal ma yin// de skad tshig du glengs pa'i tshe// bde chen dbyings su sangs rgyas par// ston pa rgyal mchog nyid kyis mkhyen// de nas rgyal po rdzogs sangs rgyas// btsun mo'i tshogs dang gnyis med pas// rnam gnyis glengs
6b2(rgyud 'grel): don thugs chung ste// gzhung don rnam pa bshad pa mdzad// rdzogs chen rtogs pa'i rnal 'byor pas// rtogs spyod rnam pa nyi shu yis// mngon rdzogs rgyal por de nyid nges// byang chub mchog tu sems bskyed pa// thog mar 'gro ba'i lam mchog yin// byang chub mchog
6b3(rgyud 'grel): ldan rnal 'byor des// chos kun nges don gtan la phab// nges pa'i don nyid rtogs pa'i tshe// ming tsam snang po'i chos rnams kun// yi ge 'khor lo mngon sangs rgyas// mngoni rdzogs yi ge de nyid laso// ting 'dzin rol mo mtha' yas 'phros// spros nyid dkyil
6b4(rgyud 'grel): 'a'akhor bsamau yas gsal// gsal byed sngags kyi yi ge brjod// de nyid thugs rtags phyag rgyar gsal// ma mthong slongs la bstan pa'i phyir// bkri dang rdul tshon bstan paces// dkyil 'khor dag la brten pa'i mi// dbang mchog sbyin pa mchog yin no//
6b5(rgyud 'grel): dbang mchog rdzogs nas tshogs la 'jug/ tshegs bsgrub yon tan bsam mi khyab// tshogs mchog rgya cher spel ba yang // man ngag snying po can gyis bya// tshogs dus stong pa glu yis bya// gal te zhi bas mi 'dul na// rdo rje khro bo'i dkyil 'khor spro// khros pa'i
6b6(rgyud 'grel): sngags kyi bskur ston nas// dkyil 'khor nying du bkod par bya// de nyid la ni mchod pa 'bul// ni khri rab 'byam mchod pa'i tshe// sdom la gnas pa shin tu gces// dam tshig ldan po'i skyes bu de// rnam bzhi las kyi gzhan don bya// khros pa'i grub bstong pa bya//
7a1(rgyud 'grel): don dam kun rdzob byang chub sems// rnam pa gnyis su ston pas gsung // rmad du byung ba'i byang chub sems// sangs rgyas kun gyi gsang ba'i thugs// ye shes lnga'i rang bzhin ni// skye 'gag gnas dmigs 'gro 'ong rnams// don
7a2(rgyud 'grel): dam med las kun sgrib yod// don dam kun sgrib dbyer med don// dam pa'i don du bde gshegs gsungs// brjod med de nyid brjod pa'i tshe// nyid kyi rtse bzungs 'khor lo mnyes// don ma rtogs dang snying rje dang // don mdzad kun rdzob rnam pa gsum// rgyal
7a3(rgyud 'grel): rgyal mo 'khor bcas pas// rtogs dka'i gseng po rnam bzhir brjod// ye nas rtogs dka'i gsang ba dang // sna tshogs chos rnams thams cad kyi// rang bzhin de nyid gsang bu dang // rang rang chos kyi ngo bo nyid// mtshan nyid so so rtogs pa gsang // snod
7a4(rgyud 'grel): min gzhan la mi bstan gsang // ma rtogs don nyid brjod pa yin// chos kun rang bzhin sangs rgyas kyang // de nyid ma rtogs 'khrul 'khor khyab// zhen pa bzlog phyir snying rje bskyed// rang bzhin gsang ba bstan pa'i phyir// chos sgo bsam yas spros pa
7a5(rgyud 'grel): mdzad/ rang bzhin med pa'i chos nyid las// 'gro ba 'khrul 'khor snang ba yang // bdag 'dzin tsam las ma rtogs pa// 'khrul 'khor dngos nyid ga la yod// dper na mkha' la mdud 'dor 'dra// bdag 'dzin 'ching ba dam po yang // bcings byed bcing
7a6(rgyud 'grel): phyag la yod// de bas lhun grub dkyil 'khor che// de nyid bstan phyir 'i shad pa mdzad// de skad bde gshegs rgyal mchog gos// 'khor rnams bde gshegs dkyil 'khor lo// 'gro ba rnams kyi mched du gsung // sems bskyed pa'i lo'u ste/
7b1(rgyud 'grel): gnyis pa'o// / bstan la dbab par bya ba dang // bstan la phab pa gnyis su bshad// dbab pa sprul skus 'dul bstan la// nges pa'i don gyi bstan la phebs ces bya// gang las gang 'apon gang du ci byed dang // gang gis don mdzad yin te rnam pa lnga'o//
7b2(rgyud 'grel): gang las rgyal mchog sku gsung las// thugs rje rig pa'i thub drug mthon// gang du las kyi 'bras bu ste// stong gsum cig la chags tshul drug/ sprul sku cig gi zhing du grags// drug gi 'jig rten de nyid na// gling rnams bye ba phrag brgya yin// sprul pa bye ba
7b3(rgyud 'grel): phrag brgyar snang // gling rnams re rer sprul pa re re yang // 'gro drug las kyi drug du snang ba yin// dper na bar snang zla ba cig shar bas// 'dzam bu gling gi chu rnams kun du chu zlar snang // chu cig nang na snang ba'i zla ba yang // 'gro ba so sos bltas na rang re'i mdun na
7b4(rgyud 'grel): snang / de bzhin sbrul sku cig la gling rnams snang // gling rnams cig las 'gro ba drug du snang // thA dad de ku ni sprul pa cig du grags// de 'dra'i stong gsum mtha' yas mu med na// de 'dra'i sprul pa re res 'gro don de ltar mdzad// ci mdzad 'dul ba rnam pa bzhis
7b5(rgyud 'grel): gang gis 'gro ba ldang na mdzad// mngon gsum rdzu 'phrul bsod nams rnam rig pa bzhis// thig lnga'i rigs can 'gro lnga'i don rnams mdzad// mngon gsum 'khya bas sangs rgyas mdzad pa sngon// rdzu 'phrul mthun mongs ma yin sngon shes drug/ bsod nams
7b6(rgyud 'grel): kun du sku dang gsung thugs zhal// bsam gyis mi khyab grangs med phyogs bcur snang // rigs pas theg dang brgya bcur bzhir gsungs pa// 'dul ba'i dbang gi thig lnga'i rigs dang sbyar// nyon mongs rten por sgo mang dus gsum gsungs// gzugs 'dzin gyi
8a1(rgyud 'grel): nang rten 'brel 'dul rnams la// mi dang lha dang nyan thos rang rgyal bstan// 'khrul 'dogs las 'bras chung mi zas 'dul la// byang chub sems dpa'i theg pas phan 'dogs so// las 'bras mi rtog rtogs pa'i blo ldan la// bla med rdo
8a2(rgyud 'grel): theg pa'i mthar thug go/ de kun 'dul ba'i dbang ste bkri ba'i don// de dag nges par bstan la dbab pa yang // bde gshegs rgyal bas 'gro ba'i ched brjod pa// lha mi nyan thos rang rgyal theg pa la// mi rigs gzugs 'dzin phyi nang rten 'brel 'khor// mi mthun
8a3(rgyud 'grel): bde dang sdug bsngal sna tshogs kyang // 'khrul pa de nyid snang ba ma gtogs par// rang bzhin dbyings las nyams pa med ces gsung // bden pa gnyis rtogs byang chub sems dpa' yang // gnyis tshul bdag dang bdag gis gzhan med de// rnam dag chos kyi dbying
8a4(rgyud 'grel): las gnyis su med// bdag gzhan rtog pa tsam ste don du med// log rgyud nyid rtog pa rang sems skad cig ma// skad cig gzhi rtsa med pas chos kyi dbyings// bla med dngos grub gzhan nas re ba yang // bdag dang gzhan du rtog pa'i rgyun yin pas// nyid la nyid spyod nyid
8a5(rgyud 'grel): la nyid dbang bskur// theg pa'i khyad par rnam lngar bstan pa yang // 'bras bu rdzogs chen theg pa cig tu gnas// bsod nams bsam gyis mi khyab snang ba dang // khyad par sngon shes drug du snang ba yang // bsod nams rgyu las grub pa ma yin te// de nyid yang dag
8a6(rgyud 'grel): rtogs pa'i byin rlabs las// rang bzhin med las cir yang grub// sangs rgyas mdzad pa rims par ston pa yang // 'gro ba 'dul ba'i thabs las ma rtogs pa// sangs rgyas zhes bye mya ngan ci la 'da'// chos kyi dbyings kyang nub par mi 'gyur ro// 'di skad bcad
8b1(rgyud 'grel): babazhes kyang de phyir brjod// zhing khams kun du grags pa'i snying po 'di// sde snod kun dang rgyud kun 'byung ba'i yum// de phyir snying po zhes su rgyal bas gsungs// de dag bstan la 'bebs pas nges pa'ang yin// de phyir bstan pa yongs kyi 'byung gnas yin// nyon mongs
8b2(rgyud 'grel): brgyad khri ba ni stong snyen po ru// ming dang tshig du sgo rnams bstan pa yang // 'gro ba 'dul ba'i dbang tsam ma rtogs po// ston ming tshig la dngos po ga la yod// de kun tha sdang yin zhes rgyal bas mched du brjod// de nas nyid kyi gsang ba yi// dkyil 'khor kun gyi
8b3(rgyud 'grel): gsang ba 'di// sku gsung rdo rje nyid las byung // a ni skyed med shes rab dbyings// ha~M ni thabs mchog cho 'phrul rol// srid gsum 'khrul 'khor thams cad kun// log rtog nyid las ci yang min// log rtog bzhi rtsa med dbyings yin// rang rig ye shes bdag
8b4(rgyud 'grel): med thugs// ba byed med pas kun dbang sgyur// de nyid yon tan zhing khams las// gzhan med rang rig de ltar snang // rdul snyed sprul pa bsam yas kyis// 'dul ba'i dbang gi gsungs pa kun// bla med nges pa'i don 'di ru// 'dus par bde gshegs nyid
8b5(rgyud 'grel): kyis mkhyen// bstan la phab pa'i le'u ste/ gsum pa'o// / yi ge 'khor lo'i dkyil 'khor 'di// gang las ji ltar gang phyung phyung ba'i 'bru// don bshad gsang ba'i dkyil 'khor phyung ba dang // rnam pa 'di drug yi ge 'khor lo bshang /
8b6(rgyud 'grel): gang las byung ba rnam bzhir shes bya ste// dgongs dang ting 'dzin ming dang 'byung khungs so// bde gshegs mnyam nyid dgongs pa gcig tu gyur// mnyam nyid rdo rje dbyings kyi dkyil 'khor du// chos kun yi nas sangs rgyas ting 'dzin bstan// kun rdzob mi btsam
9a1(rgyud 'grel): yi ge 'phreng zhes bya// byung khungs ston pa'i sku gsung thugs rdo rje// ji ltar a byung a las ming tshogs byung // a dkar bzhi las a rnams phyogs bcur 'phros// phyogs kun gsal nas slar 'dus gzhi la thims// 'phros pas 'grib med
9a2(rgyud 'grel): sa pas 'phel med pa// spros pas gzhan don sdus pas bdag gi don// a 'dang ka la sogs pa bzhi bcu gnyis// shin tu phra ba'i tshul gyi spro bsdu ba// mi 'grib mi 'phel bdag gzhan don du bshad// a nyid rgyu ste ming tshogs 'bras bur gsungs// sku gsung
9a3(rgyud 'grel): thugs kyi klong nas a 'byung ste// a ni khongs nas 'byung bas skye ba med// a las 'od zer 'gur gyi gsang bar 'khyil// 'od 'phros ka la sogs pa 'bru lngar shar// oM'i 'od zer zla kham ljags la 'khyil// 'od 'phros rtsa la sogs pa 'bru lngar shar// e'i
9a4(rgyud 'grel): 'od zer ljags kyi rtser 'phros pas// cho 'phrul ta la sogs pa 'bru bcur shar// zhal gyi sgo mor a'i 'od 'phros pas// cho 'phrul pa la sogs pa 'bru lnga yin// a las phyi rol yul la 'od 'phros pas// cho 'phrul yi ge nyi shu sku las 'phros// ya ni bin pa
9a5(rgyud 'grel): las byub Ta ni sku khab las// ra ni rtag zur la ni dpungs pa las ni byung // thugs kha'i 'od las sha byung phyag 'thil las ni Sha// mdzod spu 'od las sa byung zhabs 'thil gnyis las ha// gsang ba'i 'od zer las ni cho 'phrul kA ru sha ra// spyan gnyis las ni tshe
9a6(rgyud 'grel): phrul i gnyis shar// sman gnyis las ni cho 'phrul u gnyis shar// tshems gnyis las ni 'od 'phros e gnyis shar// shangs gnyis las ni 'ong 'phros oM gnyis shar// skyes bu'i spri gtsug 'od 'phros mgo zhes pa zer// 'khru tshang lte ba las ni 'od
9b1(rgyud 'grel): 'bros shad ces bya// skyes bu chen po 'tshegs ma'i bod las thig ces pa// gar byung bzhi bcu rtsa lnga de nyid yin// phyung ba'i nus 'thu 'jig rten bsam yas g.yo// don bshad rnam pa gnyis su shes pa ste// spyi dang rang gi mtshan nyid don bshad pa'o// spyi'i don ni rnam dgur
9b2(rgyud 'grel): sabya ste// don dang chi ba las dang mtshan nyid drangaso// dbye ba rang bzhin cho 'phral nges tshig go// don ni bden pa gnyis su shes pa ste// a ni don dam mtha' gnyis dbus mi dmigs// kun rdzob ming tsam yi ge 'phreng ba nyid// chos kun sgyu ma ming tsam nyid la gnas//
9b3(rgyud 'grel): a las yo ge'i tshogs 'byung sgra dang bcas// ming tsam tshig gi bsdus pa'i mngon rdzogs nyid// rdzogs sangs rgyas te yi ge'i che bar gsungs// las ni ya mtshan bzhi bcu rtsa lnga yis// ming tshig don mtshon sna tshogs smra zhing ston// mtshan nyid don dam dbyings
9b4(rgyud 'grel): las dmigs med kyang // kha dog ming dbyibs rol pa sprul cing ston// rnam grangs dkyil 'khor bzhi bcu rtsa lnga nyid// re re la yang sku gsung thugs su bshad// thugs ni rgyu nyid a yis kun la khyab// sku ni so so'i kha dog dbyibs su ldan// gsung ni sgra yi ming gis
9b5(rgyud 'grel): thams cad bsdus// de phyir phyogs bcu ra rgyal ba'i sku gsung thugs// bzhi bcu rtsa lnga gsum 'phror 'gyur zhes gsung // dbye ba lus dang yan lag gnyis su dbye// lus ni mgo nas kwa'i bar du rdzogs// yan lag 'drin dang grags po bzhi gnyis yin// rang bzhin
9b6(rgyud 'grel): sems nyid yi ge'i rang bzhin ste// sems dang yi ge'i dngos po yod ma yin// cho 'phrul mtshan ma dbyings las sna tshogs sprul// rgyal ba'i sku gsung thugs kyi cho 'phrul rnams// yi ge mthu'i 'gug cing bed nus na// 'jig rten cho 'phrul gzhan lta smos ci dgos// nges
10a1(rgyud 'grel): tshig bris pa'i phyir na yi ge ste// mtshan med dbyings la dbyings kyi bris pa yang // a nyid dbyings las sna tshogs 'byung phyir ro// rang gi mtshan nyid so sor bshad pa ni// bzhi bcu rtsa drug rang bzhin las rnams yin// mgo'i
10a2(rgyud 'grel): zhin ma nor de nyid rnam pa gsum// las ni lam yin rtog pa rnam pa bzhi// thig gi rang bzhin shes rab rnam pa gsum// las ni nga nyid mtshon bar ming du smra// shad ni rang bzhin thabs chen snyan bsgrub bzhi// las ni mtshon pa'i ming rnams
10a3(rgyud 'grel): su gcod// a'i rang bzhin ske mad dbu ma'i ngang // las ni de bzhin nyid mtshon dag mnyam bzhi// a mgo thig bshad ting 'dzin bzhir bshad ngo // de bzhin nyid kun snang sgra rdzogs zhes pa// des ni sngon rdzogs phyag rgya'i rgyu bzhir nges// tha
10a4(rgyud 'grel): sa bde gshegs lnga rdzogs phung po lnga'i// rang bzhin sgyu 'phral yin te las ni rigs lnga'o// tha sogs lnga ni btsun mo'i dbyings rnams lnga// rang bzhin dra ba las ni 'byung lde nyid// sgra 'phrul dra ba zhes kyang rno dang gzungs la grags// ka la
10a5(rgyud 'grel): sa pa sems dpa'i yi ge lnga// rang bzhin thugs sna las ni rnam shes khams lnga yin// tsa sogs yul gyi sems bzhi rigs dang rnams lnga po// rang bzhin sku ste las ni yul gyi khams lnga yin// sa la sogs pa sems dpa'i yi ge lnga'i//
10a6(rgyud 'grel): rang bzhin gsungs te las ni dbang po'i khams lnga yin// ya la sogs pa reg ma'i yi ge bzhi// rang bzhin dag pa bzhi ste las ni dus rnams bzhi// sha la sogs pa rogs ma'i yi ge bzhi// rang bzhin med pa bzhi ste las ni mtha' bzhi 'joms// kwa
10b1(rgyud 'grel): ni sdung pa'i rang bzhin thugs kyi thugs sde las ni ye shes yin// si la sogs pa sprul pa'i yi ge rnams drug go/ sbrul pa'i rang bzhin pasam las rdul snyeng las n-i rigs drug 'dul// yo na srid dbang dag pa'i rgyal bab ya~M ga ste// rang banin byang chub seMn/
10b2(rgyud 'grel): ste las ni thams cad 'jig/ oM ni sdud pa kun tu bzang mo'i yi ge ste// rang bzhin chos rnams thams cad las ni kun bzhi yin// las dang rang bzhin 'brel pa'i 'khor lo'i tshogs tshon 'di// re re la yang sku gsung thugs kyi man Da la rdzogs pa'i 'phreng // yi
10b3(rgyud 'grel): ge 'khor lo tshogs chen zhes su brjod// yig 'bru gsang ba'i dkyil 'khor ni// gang byung gang las ji ltar byung // byung ba'i 'bras bu nyid dang bzhi// gang byung bder gshegs thams cad kyi// rab tu gsang ba'i dkyil 'khor yin// gang las sku gsung rdo rje
10b4(rgyud 'grel): las// ji ltar yab yum dgyes sprin las// a re gsal a las yig 'bru tshegs// de la sngon rdzogs skur gsal ba// yum gyi mkha' la rdzogs par rol// lhag pa'i ting 'dzin zhes su grags// de nyid las ni phyi rol gyi// dkyil 'khor 'don par
10b5(rgyud 'grel): rgyal bas gsungs// b+ha ga dkyil 'khor ling ga e// 'dus ma byas nyid rdo rje las// 'dus byas rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor tshogs// 'byin pa'i dam tshig 'da' mi 'gyur// ci phyir thabs dang shes rab kyi// rgyu rkyen tshogs pa'i mthu chen yin de'i 'bras bu yi ge nyid//
10b6(rgyud 'grel): rgyal ba mngon par rdzogs pa'i sku// dkyil 'khor nyid du lhun gyis grub// yi ge 'phreng ba bkod pa'i le'u ste bzhi pa'o// / sna tshogs sgyu 'phrul spros pa 'di// gang las gang spros thabs dang mnyes pa bzhi// gang las sgyu 'phrul dkyil 'khor bkod
11a1(rgyud 'grel): pa las// gang spros ting 'dzin rnam par spros pa 'di// thabs ni bdun gyis bsgrub thabs sdebs bshad pa// ting nge 'dzin dang rdzogs dang thun mong dang // dpe dang sgra dang grags gsal mchog rdzogs 'gyur// ting 'dzin de bzhin nyid dang
11a2(rgyud 'grel): kun snang sgra yin te// ting 'dzin de bzhin rang sems mtshan nyid ni// gang gis mi shes chos kyi dbyings mi shes// dmigs med mi shes rtag chad 'jig mi 'gyur// de phyir rang sems dbyings nyid thabs kyi rgyu// dngos po rnam pa brgyad sogs gang yang
11a3(rgyud 'grel): min/ min pa de nyid de bzhin nyid ces bya// de nyid gsal bar sgom pa thabs kyi rgyu// kun khyab snying rje rang bzhin kun snang yin// rgyu ni sems nyid a'i rang bzhin ste// a nyid yid bzhin rin chen sprin dang mtshungs// a las sgyu 'phrul bzhi bcu rtsa gnyis
11a4(rgyud 'grel): 'byung // de nyid thabs las thabs byung thobs bsam las// thabs nyid dra ba'i dkyil 'khor rdzogs pa'i sku// rdzogs pa'i yig 'bru drug mtshan sngon rdzogs sku// don dam dbyer med kun rdzob pa dad pa'i// nang gi rnam shes nang gi dbang po dang // phyi rol su
11a5(rgyud 'grel): gyi rnam pa thams cad kun// bsam yas dkyil 'khor kun bzang phyag rgyar rol// de nyid sgyu 'phrul mngon rdzogs rgyal por nges// dngos grub thun mongs rnam pa sna tshogs kun// glang chen myos 'dra'i sems ni ting nge 'dzin gyi btul nas su// sgyu
11a6(rgyud 'grel): 'brul sngags dang phyag rgya rab tu bstan pas nas// thun mong dngos grub ya mtshan 'di kun 'a grub// phyogs dus rgyal ba'i dkyil 'khor grub nas/ rgyal ba'i dpal// nyi shu rtsa gcig ting 'dzin mthu yis grub// dper na sgron me gser 'gyur sman
11b1(rgyud 'grel): kyi dug gsel dang // rangs las gser 'gyur dug las sman 'gyur ltar// ye shes rang snang ming tshig gzugs sogs las// yong bzhin dngos grub ji ltar sbyar bas 'grub// bla ma mchod ldan rtogs gsal dam tshig ldan// sngags shes phyag rgyur shes
11b2(rgyud 'grel): shing yo byad lnga ldan na// thun mong mchog gi dngos grub yod par rgyal bas gsung // de nyid mi ldan dngos grub ming de de nyid rlag par 'gyur// de dag thob pa'i rgyu dang mi thob gags zhes bshad// mchog de nyid ni rgyal ba'i thugs chung dngos grub snying po ste// mi zad
11b3(rgyud 'grel): 'phel 'grib med pa yid bzhin mdzod dang 'dra// dngos med ting nge 'dzin las dngos po yi ge sbyin// mchog gi rnam pa sna tshogs ji ltar 'dod 'byung 'gyur// dngos med dngos nyid rtog pa'i ting 'dzin mchog gi mthus// dbang sgyur bder gshegs kun gyi bdag nyid de
11b4(rgyud 'grel): yin no// de skad gsung bas 'khor gyi bde gshegs thams cad kun// mchog dang thun mong gzigs mos mnyes par 'gyur// sgyu 'phrul sgrub pa ting nge 'dzin gyi le'u ste lnga pa'o// / de nas sgyu 'phrul dkyil 'khor spros bshad pa// gang gis
11b5(rgyud 'grel): gang du gang spros ji ltar 'gyur// gsang ba'i dkyil 'khor spros te rnam lnga yin// gang gis ston pa bde gshegs thams cad kyang // rang bzhin gcig dang du med bden gnyis dbyer med pas// gang du 'jig rten drug gi bsam yas thams cad la// rgyal ba
11b6(rgyud 'grel): nyid kyi sku gsung che ba'i dkyil 'khor 'byin par dgongs// gang spros rtogs dang spyod pa gnyis su bshad// rtog pa ji ltar gang rtags gang gis rtags na ngon 'byung ba'o// de ltar phyogs bzhi dbus lngar ye shes lngar rtags te// gang rtags bsam yas 'jig rten
12a1(rgyud 'grel): lhun grub nyid bar// gang gis bde gshegs rdzogs pa rtog pa'i rnal 'byor bde gshegs mtshungs// brtags nas don 'byung kun 'byung dkyil 'khor chen por spyod// mdzad sbyong rnam pa bcu yis lhun gyis grub// bzhal
12a2(rgyud 'grel): las brgyan dang gdan khri bzhugs tshul dang // bzhugs gnas thugs mtshan sku mdog tshul dgu dang // 'od zer 'phro dang khyab pa che ba'o// gzhal yas 'khor 'khyud gra khams gru bzhi sgo 'khyud bzhi// brgyan ni rol mo'i sprin phung lha mchog bzhi bcu
12a3(rgyud 'grel): bas sa sa @ la bya chubs mas drug/ sprul ma nus hU~M 'i sgyus da sgrubs rgyal// banas ni 'khyi thabs pargyal rtsi la ma bsdu/ blo
12a4(rgyud 'grel): bzhi la rigs bzhi yul bzhi zung bzhi pa khril// grwa bzhir dbang po bzhi dang dus bzhi zungs 'khril nas// 'khyams yi thungab drug bya byed nub dang sher// sgo bzhir 'joms pa 'joms ma de bzhin du// thugs mtshan rgyal po phag drug phyag rgya drug/ drug lnga sum cu
12a5(rgyud 'grel): ye shes rtags su bstan// rnam shes rdo rje ral gri 'khor lo g.yas// dril bu rin chen pad+ma g.yon na 'dzin// gzugs ni 'khor lo ral gri rdo rje g.yas// dril bu pad+ma rin chen g.yon na 'dzin// tshor ba rin chen 'khor lo rdo rje g.yos// dril bu pad+ma ral gri g.yon
12a6(rgyud 'grel): na 'dzin// 'du shes pad+ma 'khor lo rdo rje g.yas// dril bu rin chen ral gri g.yon na 'dzin// 'du byed ral gri 'khor lo rdo rje g.yas// dril bu rin chen pad+ma g.yon na 'dzin// rgyal mo g.yas kyi dang po dril bu ste// g.yon pa rang rtags bzhi bzhi rno dang 'thun// shes rab
12b1(rgyud 'grel): yum yang drug lnga sum cur bshad// ut+pal klu shing po ti pad+ma dkar// dri spros me tog mar me dbang bani dus bzhi yin// shis bzhi myu gu ral gri pad+ma rdo rje// mdzes 'phreng gi bang gar ni yul bzhi'o// bi wang sreg par go cha bo ti dang // rin chen sgrom dang me chu thub par grags
12b2(rgyud 'grel): mnyam bzhag ting 'dzin phyag rgya yid chos yin// 'joms ni mgo dang thod sbrul rdo rje rgya gram gnon// lcags kyu zhags pa lcags sgrog dril 'joms mtshan// kun kyang zhal gcig phyag gnyis mdzes pa'i yo byad 'dzin// mdog ni rtso bzung rang rig kha dog lnga//
12b3(rgyud 'grel): gcig la yang lnga lnga nyi shu rtsa lngar brtags// thub drug mdog ni cis 'dul nges pa med// yid chos 'thing ka nam mkha'i mdog du bstan// gzhan rnams rigs kyi bye brag dag gis dbye// tshul ni bsnyen lcags 'khril ldem gzhon chas can// gsal la 'tsher
12b4(rgyud 'grel): la lhun sdug gzi byin ldan// 'joms pa 'joms ma rtogs tshul dgu po 'od zer 'khyil cing brgyan yang 'khyil pa ste// 'od zer lnga la nyi shu rtsa lngar 'phros shing 'khyol// stong rtsa lnga bcur phyogs bcur 'phros gyur kyang // stong phrag bcu dang brgya phrag lnga yin no// /
12b5(rgyud 'grel): 'byung ba'i gnas kyi tha dad brtsis 'gyur na// bcu po gcig la'ang spyan drug snyan drug ste// de bzhin shangs ljags sku dang thugs mtshan drug/ sum cu drug la nyi shu lnga lngar 'bros// spyi ni stong phrag dgu ni bshad pa yin// sum cu gnyis po gcig la'ang bcu
12b6(rgyud 'grel): dang gnyis// de bzhin spros na stong dgu brgya drag drug/ stong phrag ba co brgyad brgya phrag drug ces bya// de las phyogs bcur spros na khri phrag ni// bco brgyad stong phrag drug du bshad ba yin// de ltar phyogs bcur 'gro drug don byed che// bye ba phrag khrig drug tu
13a1(rgyud 'grel): 'phro zhing 'khyil// yan lag nyin lag tshul dgu'i brgyan rnams las// legs par rtsis na rtsis las 'das pa yin// dkyil 'khor bsam yas zhes kyang de la bya// rgyan ni dbu brgyan snyan cha 'gur chu dpung brgyan dang // phyag
13a2(rgyud 'grel): rngub zhabs rngub sku rigs se mo do// rin chen rgyu las grub ste dbyings dang ye shes brgyan// bcu po dag la yang dbu brgyan rigs lnga ste// sum cu gnyis la bdag po re re yin// bcu po lnga ni snyan cha drug drug ste// gzhan yang gnyis gnyis 'gur chu
13a3(rgyud 'grel): gsum dang gtsog/ dpung brgyan phyag rngub drug dang gnyis de bzhin// kun la zhabs rngub gnyis gnyis brgyan par bshad// sku rigs se mo don re re'o// bcu po re re la yang sum cu ste// gzhan dag la ni bcu dang gnyis kyis brgyan// spyir ni drug brgya/
13a4(rgyud 'grel): da ni brgya bcu bzhi// des na brgyan gyi dkyil 'khor ldan gyis grub// khyab pa'i che ba name mkhas gar khyab pa'i// bsam yas dkyil 'khor gyis ni khyab par grags// drug cu rtsa gnyis sman gyis drug cu rtsa gnyis mtha' la gzigs// de bzhin snyan rnams
13a5(rgyud 'grel): kyis ni drug cu rtsa gnyis mtha' gsan cing // shangs nas drug cu rtsa gnyis sprul pa 'gyed// ljags kyis drug cu rtsa gnyis rdul thabs 'chad// sku ni drug cu rtsa gnyis 'dul ba mdzad// thugs ni drug cu rtsa gnyis phyin ci ma log mkhyen// sum brgya bdun
13a6(rgyud 'grel): cu rtsa gnyis dgongs pa bsam mi khyab// dkyil 'khor bsam yas lhun grub ces kyang de la bya'o// ji ltar gyur na 'di ltar spros pa'i tshe// 'jig rten mtha' yas mu med thams cad kun// rdul snyed brjod kyis mi lang dkyil 'khor rdzogs// khams gsum
13b1(rgyud 'grel): sems can gcig gis rgyud la yang // de snyed dkyil 'khor bsam yas lhun gyis grub// ting 'dzin gsang ba'i dkyil 'khor spros pa yang // sku gsung thugs kyi rdo rje nyid las 'byung // dkyil 'khor dmigs par bya ba byed pa mi dmigs te// dpag
13b2(rgyud 'grel): cing bsam 'das brjod med dkyil 'khor de nyid rang rig yin// de nyid mnyam dang mi mnyam chos la khyab tsam nyid na khyab pa med// khyab med de nyid khyab pa'i dbyings te rang rig kun la gsal// dkyil 'khor bsam yas rnam par spros kyang spro pa rdul tsam med//
13b3(rgyud 'grel): dkyil 'khor spros pa'i le'u ste drug pa'o// snying po 'byung dang byin bsdu rnam pa gnyis// snying po 'byung ba rnam pa drug yin to// gzhal yas bskyed dang sku bskyed spyan drangs dang // dngos grub blang dang grangs dang gsang dbang bskur//
13b4(rgyud 'grel): sku gsung thugs nyid rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor las// gzhal yas sa bon yi ge bruM yin te// gtsug tor 'khor lo smon lam rang gi sngags// sngags kyis tshogs kyis gzhal yas rdzogs par bsgom// dper na sa bon 'byung bas bskyed las 'bras bu smin
13b5(rgyud 'grel): tshul du// sa bon yig 'bru las ni 'bras bu sngags kyi rdzogs// sa bon bzhi bcu rtsa gnyis rgyu yin te// sngags tshig sku bskyed rkyen gyi sngags ces bya// e he ba ga b+han ma hA ka ru ni ka tri sha ho// sa ma ya s+t+wa~M/ dza hUM baM ho/ ces spyan yang drangs/ oM badz+ra sa ma
13b6(rgyud 'grel): ye oM ces pa la sogs pas bskul ba yin// dngos grub tshe na tshig bshad sngags bcas brjod// rgyal ba'i sku gsung thugs dang yon tan dang // 'phrin las ngag dang lnga po re re yang // rnam pa lnga lnga mkhas pas bshad pa de// de rtogs dang bdag nyid mnyam
14a1(rgyud 'grel): bar sbyor ba yin// sku lnga rmad du byung bar bstan pa ni// chos sku longs spyod rdzogs dang sprul sku dang // mngon par byang chub rdo rje'i sku dang lnga// rtag tu mkha' 'dod bde sbed zas sbyin 'dod// mngon pa rtswa byang nub lnga sogs 'dus ma byas//
14a2(rgyud 'grel): gsung lnga rmad du byung bar bston pa ni// yi ge med rigs longs spyod rdzogs gsung dang // tshangs dbyangs yan lag gsungs dang rdo rje gsung // brjid bral rtogs med me long gzugs lta zhing // yan lag drug cu brjod sgra 'dus ma khyim// thugs lnga rmad du byung shes
14a3(rgyud 'grel): brjod pa ni// mi rtag ci yang gsol bde ba che// 'gro ba sgrol dang rdo rje'i thugs dang lnga// me long mi rtog kun mkhyen mnyam pa nyid// nan tan las te ma skyes chos kyi dbyings// yon tan rmad du byung ba lngar bstan pa// zhing khams gzhal yas 'od zer gdan khri dang // che ba'i
14a4(rgyud 'grel): sa spyong bsam gyis mi khab pa// thugs rje sprul cing bams pa'i khyim du bsdad// btang snyoms gzar 'phros sgrib bsrel yon tan brtags// khar zhugs dag pa lnga sprong re 'dod rgong // 'brin las rmad du byung ba lngar bstan pa// zhi rgyas dbang dang mngon spyod
14a5(rgyud 'grel): lhun grub pa// ma skyes kun tu bzang po rang bzhin mngon du gyur// rgyu rkyen 'bad rtsol med pa ye nas yin// sdug bkren log lta kheng sems thams cad 'jom// de dag gcig la'ang de ltar brtsis gyur na// thug pa med par mi zad brgyan du snang // rmad byung tshon po
14a6(rgyud 'grel): zhes kyang de la bya'o// grags pas bsam las gsung gi dkyil 'khor gyis// bsam yas dkyil 'khor dag du rab tu grags// gsang ba'i dbang ni rnam pa bzhi yin te// gang gis gang zhig gang la ji ltar bskur// gang gis rgyal po rgyal mo rtse gzungs kyis//
14b1(rgyud 'grel): gsang ba de nyid thugs la bsdu bya'i phyir// gang zhig gis ni lhag pa'i sbyor sems kyis// lha mo brgyad kyis sbyor ba brda' smos te// sa ma ya sI yum gyis bskul ba yin// bdag ni dam tshig bstan ma zhes ni de la bya// sa ma ya ho tso bos lan byin te// khyod ni dam
14b2(rgyud 'grel): tshig dga' ma zhes su bya// ra ho ha ni brtsol bskul ba ste// bdag ni chags pa can pas chags mdzod che'o// ra ga ya mi bskul ba'i lan yin te// khyod ni chags pas chags pa'i gnas ces pa'o// smon dang 'jug dang ldangs dang gnas pa'i// byang chub rnam pa
14b3(rgyud 'grel): zhir yang mkhas pas bshad// dzA ni lcags kyus gzungs nyid 'dren pa yin// hUM ni zhags pa'i phyag rgyas 'khyud pa mdzad// paM ni sgrog sde dbang po bsdam pa yin// ho ni dril bus mnyes par byed pa'i brda'// phyag rgya bzhi zhes kyang ni mkhas pas bshad// pra be
14b4(rgyud 'grel): shas ni pad+ma'i sgo phye yin// a be shas ni 'bebs pa zhes su bshad// pu ke zhes bya bde bar rdur pa'o// tsit+ta byang chub sems kyi thig le nyid// g.yo dang reg dang myongs dang myongs zhes pa/ reg pa rnam pa bzhir yang mkhas pas bshad// gang la yid chos gtso
14b5(rgyud 'grel): babazungs de nyid la// ji ltar byang chub sems kyi dkyil 'khor de// gsang ba bsdu phyir gnyis med dbyings su stim// gsang ba bsdang po yin zhes de phyir brjod// ye shes byin sdu zhes bya ba// gang las gang byung ji ltar gyur pa dang // gsung gi rang bzhin
14b6(rgyud 'grel): stan te rnam pa bzhi// gang las sku gsung thugs kyi sgyu 'phral las// ye shes lnga dang sku gsung thugs nyid dang // chags dang mtshang pa byin rlobs snying po 'byung // ji ltar ye shes kyis ni/ thims par 'gyur// sku gsung thugs su dbang bskur gsal
15a1(rgyud 'grel): bar 'gyur// chags dang mchod pa shin tu gsal bar 'gyur// rang bzhin ngo mtshar sangs rgyas kun gyi gsung // sgra dang ming tshogs kun las 'das kyis kyang // tshig gi sna tshogs sgra rnams go bar bsgrags// de phyir ljags nyid drug
15a2(rgyud 'grel): turtsa gnyis yin// de dag gcig la'ang 'gro drug so so'i skad// drag po de nyid phyogs bcur bsgrags snang bas// gsung dbangs yan lag drug cu de la ba// 'gro drug gcig la'ang sgra skang pa dad pas// bsam gyis mi khyab sgra skang pa dang grags// de phyir
15a3(rgyud 'grel): gsung gi dkyil 'khor mtha' yas mchog/ ces gsung / sngags kyi le'u ste/ bdun pa'o// / phyag rgya'i dkyil 'khor bshad bya ba// gang gis ji ltar gang gsungs pa// gang gis rgyal ba nyid kyis gsungs// ji ltar yan lag
15a4(rgyud 'grel): dkyil 'khor de// dbu ni bang gshegs rigs yin te// lag g.yas rdo rje mi stod pa// lag g.yon rin chen sems dpa'i rigs// rkang g.yon chos kyi sems pa ste// rkang g.yas las kyi sems dpa'o// dkyil 'khor nyid du lhun gyis grub// de ni lhun
15a5(rgyud 'grel): grub phyag rgya yin// lag sor g.yas g.yon yab yum bcu// nyi zla'i 'od bkod 'bru byin rlabs// gung gnyis la ni hUM dang chu// 'dzub mo gnyis la oM dang lang // dbang po gnyis las dang ma// chung ngun la ni oM dang spyi// spo bo gnyis la ha dang ta// de ltar
15a6(rgyud 'grel): byin byos rlabs bya ste// phyag rgya bcings par gsungs pa ying // nges pa'i tshig dang 'byung ba'i rgyu// spyi dang so so rnam pa na'o// nges tshig sgyu 'phrul phyag rgya kun rdzogs dang // don dam chos sgra byang chub mchog gi// gsang ba'ing phyag rgya ma lus rgyas btu/
15b1(rgyud 'grel): bas/ thams cad pag rgya nyid las ga la 'da'// rgyu nyid g.yas g.yon nyi Ta sbyor spro bsdu// phyi ni phyag rgya ma nges spros pa ste// oM dang ma sbyar hUM dang laM du sbyar// oM dang ta sbyar hi dang po sbyar ba// sa dang mo sbyar yab kyi spyi rgya ste// dbang mchog sbyin
15b2(rgyud 'grel): ba'i dus su bsngags po yin// yang na de nyid thul mo sbyar ba las// sgo dang dz+ha sbyar aM dang mu du sbyar// ha dang ta drA sbyar te gnyis ji bzhin// yum gyi spyi rgyu yin te las mchog dus su sbyar// so so'i ngag rgya bcu po re re la// rigs ni lnga lnga ngag dang ldan par bshad//
15b3(rgyud 'grel): gas kar bkan bde gshegs rigs yin te// rang rigs sor mo yog 'a blo rdo rje rigs// blo bsngal 'bru sdus bril bsil rin chen rags// 'khrul tshul chos la brtan pa bsgo'i rigs// de nyid byed pa las kyi rigs// sum yang thugs brtan 'dri bar gshegs
15b4(rgyud 'grel): nga'i rims// dril bsil rdo rje las 'khril las su bshad // 'dzun pa'i mdzes ldan dan chen rims pas bya// sgyum gyi rgyu bcus basmras te pad+ma'i rigs// de ltar bcings pa sa lnga bcu'i phyag rgya rdzogs// sems dpa' la sogs btsongs pa mchig rgyal// kun
15b5(rgyud 'grel): gang ya ba yum ting 'dzin phyag rgyar bya// yang na kun b.rang yab kyi sgo rgyar bzang // yus ni bal mo 'am yum gyi sgo rgya yon// rigs kyi bye brag kun la shes bya ste// de ltar brtsigs na nyis brgya ba rgya yin no// de ltar spros pas phyag rgya bsam mi khyab// phyag rgya
15b6(rgyud 'grel): spros pa'i le'u sde brgyad ba'i// / de nas mnyan ma'i dkyil 'khor bshang bya ba// gang gis ji ltar gang bshang rnam pa gsum// gang gis bde gshegs yab yum dgyes chen pos// ji ltar phyi rabs rnal 'byor snyoms 'jug phyir// gsang ba sa
16a1(rgyud 'grel): tshig bkod la snyoms zhugs nas// 'gro ba'i cheng du 'di dag bshang ba mdzad// 'dul dbang che chung rims pa'i bye brag ni// sor bzhi pa dang sor brgyad khru gang dang // khru bzhi pa dang khru ni bcu gnyis dang // bcu drug nyi shu nyi shu rtsa lngar bya// rgyang
16a2(rgyud 'grel): gas dpag tshad mthab mnyam par// che chung rims pa bcu gcig rnam grangs yin// sor bzhi dkyil 'khor 'bri dang mchod pa dang // 'jug dang slob ma dbang skur rnam bzhi yin// dgongs dang gang du gang bri ji tsam tshang // mgo ma ya dang thig gang ba dbyibs dang ni//
16a3(rgyud 'grel): gdan dang dgod thabs rgyan dgong dang ni bcu'o// dgongs pa shin tu 'phra la rab sbyangs nas// ting 'dzin las su rung zhes mkhas pas bshad// rten bcas dngos grub mi 'da' thob par bshad// gang du bdag nyid rnal 'byor rab ldan pa'i// phyag mthil nyid dang shing lob
16a4(rgyud 'grel): lta bu rung // gang 'dri rdo rje sems dpa'i dkyil 'khor nyid// dkyil 'khor kun gyi rtsa gzhi yin pas thugs// tshang ni ma nges 'dir ni sor bzhi pa'o// sku lnga las lnga yon tan lnga thugs lnga// gsum lnga rigs ni rnam lngar byin brlabs las// 'bru spros rin chen snying pa sman
16a5(rgyud 'grel): bdud rtsi// sum cu cha bsnyams 'gro ma yeng du bya// rig pas bcang bri 'am sems kyis dgod// gzugs brnyan nyid kyi dkyil 'khor zhes kyang bya// dbyibs ni rang bzhin ting 'dzin ci 'dra de nyid yin// bdan lnga 'phra mo tsam du rim pas dgod// yig 'bru phyag rgya dgos pa
16a6(rgyud 'grel): de bzhin no// rgyan ni kha rol bcos pa'i sna tshogs ras// bla rgyan 'og rgyan par rgyan mdzes pa dang // rin chen sna tshogs mdzes pa'i 'phreng bas bskor// gzugs sgra dri ro bza' btung de bzhin bskor// mchod pa phyi dang nang dang sbyin sreg dang // ting nge 'dzin dang kun
16b1(rgyud 'grel): bzang mchod pa'i sprin// gsang ba'i dkyil 'khor spyan drangs mchod pa dang // khyad par chen po'i mchod pa dang // yon tan dang ni mi dmigs bsgom// rnam pa dgu por shes par bya'o// phyi tshul glu tshig bro gar rol mo'i// tshogs mchog sbyin phung rnyed kyis mchod
16b2(rgyud 'grel): pabapar bya// nang tshul lha mo rnam pa bcu gsum rnams// ji ltar 'tshams pa'i las bzhin byin rlabs mchod// sbyin sreg rim par mchod sbyin rnams kyis mchog/ zlum po gru bzhi zla gam gru gsum dbyibs// dkar ser dmar nag bsgyur ba'i dkyil 'khor du//
16b3(rgyud 'grel): na chen mnga' gzhu thong bas mtshan// lha tshegs kun gyi zhal ni mi rnams 'bong// bza' btung las bzhi'i mchod sprin mchog yin no// zhing dang rgyas pa zhi ba'i tshogs la ste// dbang drag gnyis la 'phros pa'i dkyil 'khor ba// de yang sor bzhi pa la tsam nas su
16b4(rgyud 'grel): nam mkha' mtha' snyams bar du de bzhin pa// ting 'dzin cho 'phrul mchod pa bya ba dang // rang rig mchod sprin sna tshogs snang bas na// zhing khams longs spyod sna tshogs ldan pa ru// rin chen gzhal yas brgyan mchog mdzes spras pa// der ni lha dang lha mo
16b5(rgyud 'grel): mdzes ldan rdul rnyed dag/ blo gar glu tshig tshigs rol 'jig rten khams bkong 'bul// kun bzang mchod pas bskal ldan rtogs khyad par// blo'i khyad par dus gcig go rims kyis// chos dbyings mnyam sbyor mchod sprin phyag rgya bsgom// gsang ba'i dkyil
16b6(rgyud 'grel): 'khor rnal 'byor ma'am byin gyis brlabs// gnas lngar rigs yum lnga dang yan lal khro mo ba'i// yab yum gnyis med ldeg pa'i sbyoraro sems las// gzhal yas dkyil 'khor rdzogs pa'i dpe brjod pa// nyung 'bru nang du stong gsum shongs tshul du// yus kyi
17a1(rgyud 'grel): mkha' dbyings gnyis las brnyan mar gsal bton te// gnyis med lhag pa'i sems kyis mchod par bya// mnyes nas grub ste dam tshig mchog du gsungs// khyad par bdag nyid mchod pas rgyal bas mnyes// 'gro rnams dga' bas sbyin pa
17a2(rgyud 'grel): khyab par 'gyur// de bas thams cad mnyam pas dbyings gcig go// yon tan sgyu 'phrul dkyil 'khor bstan byas na// phyogs bcu rgyal ba'i dkyil 'khor dang // 'gro rnams bsod nams mngon thob 'gyur// bdag gi lus ngag sems dang phyi nang chos rnams kun//
17a3(rgyud 'grel): don dam mi dmigs kun rdzob dmigs g.yor tshul snang ba// dmigs med na mkha' la ni sgyu 'phrul nam mkha' bsgom// 'jug pa'i dang po bdag nyid de nas slob ma 'jug/ las rnams kun byas bdag po rigs pas 'jug/ de nas slob ma'i spyi bor dkyil 'khor bzhag
17a4(rgyud 'grel): pa slob ma 'jug pa yin// de nas dbang bskur phyir ni yon mchog dbul bar bya// bde gshegs rigs kyi rgyal srid yon yin te// rang lus rdo rje rigs te bu dang chung ma pad+ma'i rigs// nor ni rin chen gces dang yid 'thad las rigs yin// 'dod yon lnga ni lha mo'i rang
17a5(rgyud 'grel): bzhin bla ma mchod byas na// phyogs bcu'i dkyil 'khor mnyes ste bla ma de nyid dkyil 'khor na// nye ba'i rdo rje slob dpon mnyes pa smos ci dgos// slob dpon mnyes na 'di dang gzhan ma'i nyes pa dag par 'gyur// slob ma dang dang brtson 'grus brtul shugs rtog
17a6(rgyud 'grel): pa mchog ldan na// phan dang nus pa phyi nang gsang ba'i dbang rnams kyang // snod kyi rims par sbyar te chus ma zos par sbyin// thal mo rab snol sor brgyad dkyil 'khor yang ni de ltar bya// khru gang bzhi dang bcu gnyis gzhi rab mnyam te// sa gzhi gzungs phur dang ni
17b1(rgyud 'grel): thil bskung tshon byed dang // chas gos lnga dang tshang ldan sngags la yon ldan par bya// thog gang ba tsho ga la sogs mkhas pas bsgoms te bya// 'khrun bcu drug nyi shu'am nyo shu rtsa lngar 'ang de bzhin bya// dkyil 'khor de nyid ye shes lnga'i dkyil 'khor bsgoms par bya//
17b2(rgyud 'grel): rgyal ba'i gzugs dang yi ge phyag mtshan ldan pa'i gzugs kyang dgod// 'khor rnams phyag mtshan pal pa la ni yi ge dgod// rgyangs grags dpag tshad mkha' dbyings bsam yas ni// rig pas dpags te 'di yang gzugs brnyan yin zhes bya// rdul tshon bri ba'i
17b3(rgyud 'grel): dgos pa dang ni tshon dgye dang // chen po gsum gyi dgongs dang byin gyis brlabs pa dang // spyan drangs bsnyen pa pa dang dngos grub mtshan nyid dang // bsgrub pa'i yan lag yo byad dus dang 'bras bu dang // yi dam gzugs dang me tog ngor dang gags bstan pa// rnam pa
17b4(rgyud 'grel): bcu gsum gyis ni 'grub par gsungs// tshen gyi dgos pa rang bzhin ting 'dzin nyid// gsang ba ma mthong slongs la bstan pa yin// tshon sna lnga 'am nyi shu rtsa lnga nyid// dkar dmar ser ljang 'thing kha rim bzhin dgye// de nyid 'bru lnga ye shes lngar byin rlabs//
17b5(rgyud 'grel): rgyangs grags dpag tshad na mkha'i mtha' snyam pa// ting 'dzin rgya cher glo sbyangs rol mo mtha' yas mchog gi phyir// byin rlabs tha sogs yi gi 'am nyi zla'i gdan// hUM sogs snying po 'am rdo rje la sogs thugs kyi rgya// gzugs kyi sku dang yig 'bru phyag mtshan
17b6(rgyud 'grel): ldan par bya'o// de yang ting 'dzin bstan pas byin rlabs bya// chen po gsum yang dngos su bya bar dka'// 'di yang byin gyis rlabs te yid kyis dgod pa na// ya mtshan sman gyi dngos grub sangs rgyas kun gyi dam mi d+ha// sa la sogs pa gzugs brnyan lus la sogs bya
18a1(rgyud 'grel): ste/ mtshan ma'i brten du byas na rnams grol rim grub ni// rang rig ye shes kyis ni rims bzhin byin rlabs te// sems kyis sbyangs na spyi smos de nyid ye shes yin// spyan drangs phyogs dus rang bzhin thugs kyi dkyil 'khor
18a2(rgyud 'grel): las/ bsnyernyan pa'i dkyil 'khor nyid du thams cad spyan drangs pa// sgra 'phrul nyid las dza spros thams cad dgug par 'gyur// brten pa'i mtshan nyid rang rig dkyil 'khor la// gnyis med 'jug pa'i mtshan nyid rab sbyor bas// bzlas brjod byin dang
18a3(rgyud 'grel): bsdu ba'i brnyen pa yis// phyogs bcu bang gshegs dkyil 'khor thams cad kyang // mtshan ma dus dang grangs kyi brnyan pa rab tu rdzogs// dkyil 'khor nye bar gyur te mchog gi dngos grub zar mi d+ha 'grub// dngos grub mtshan nyid rang sems bsod
18a4(rgyud 'grel): nams nyid// thun mong mchog gi dngos grub yin te gzhan na med// 'khor lo sgyur rgyal dngag bsam shing dang bum pa bzang // 'dod pa'i longs spyod de dag rang sems snang las gzhan ma yin// sangs rgyas cho 'phrul ngo mtshar smad 'byung yang // rang
18a5(rgyud 'grel): sems shes rab thabs nyid de ltar de bzhin nyid las thabs kyi phyag rgyar snang ba yang // ye shes rang snang la ni ye shes rol par zad// ye shes nyid kyang sgyu ma yin par gsog/ rang snang bsod nams ye shes de nyid 'jig rten 'das sogs dngos grub bo//
18a6(rgyud 'grel): rgyal ba gzugs sku mngon 'byung ba skyob dang byin rlabs ston pa yang // rang sems rnam pa yin te gud na med// rang snang sgyu ma'i dkyil 'khor bya ba byed nus la// gzi byin byin rlabs 'gro la phan 'dogs pa// de bzhin nyid las mi gnyis 'dus ma byas pa'ang /
18b1(rgyud 'grel): mdor na rang snang sems nyid de bzhin yin phyir ro// sems nyid snang ba/ kun yang rdo rje 'dus ma bas ces mkhas pas bshad// bsgrub pa'i yan lag cho ga rnam lnga rdzogs par bya// dang po stong pa byang chub gnyis pa snying rje chen po yin// gsum pa yi ge bzhi pa la ni dam
18b2(rgyud 'grel): tshig rgya// lnga pa ni gzugs rdzogs gzugs ldan yin// yo byad gnas mchog yid 'ong dang gdan mchog nyi zla bar sogs dang // phyag mtshan rdo rje dril bu'i gzungs ma mtshan ldan dang // a mri ta sogs phyi nang 'byor pa'i yo byad ba ldan pa// snying khar ye shes sems
18b3(rgyud 'grel): dpa' bsgom de'i snying khar nyi zla'i dkyil// dam tshig phyag rgya bzhag te de stengs yig 'bru bzhag/ zla tshes spros bsdus bzlas pa'i yan lag yin// bca' lnga ldan zhing dam tshig ma nyams bsgrub la brtson na 'grub// dus ni zla ba drug dong bcu gnyis bcu drug gis//
18b4(rgyud 'grel): tshe la dbang sogs rig 'dzin rab 'bring tha ma 'grub// 'bras bu tshe dbang rigs 'dzin de nyid kyis// tshe lo bcu drug gis ni sku lnga lhun gyis grub// de ltar rig 'dzin khyad par de dag kyang // ye shes nyid la nyid snang bsam yas mchog/ zhing khams mi zad
18b5(rgyud 'grel): brgyan gyi 'khor lo ni// sprul pa bsam yas zhal mthong dang // mnyes nas chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba yin// rig 'dzin rtsal gyi khyad par de nyid kyang // tshogs gnyis mthun te ye shes rang snang ba'o// gcig dang du mar bral ba'i mtha' 'das de bzhin nyid//
18b6(rgyud 'grel): rgyal bas kyang ni gzigs pa ma yin te// rang 'byung ye shes nyid la mi gnas tshul tsam snang bar zad// log par rtog pas brtags pa kun kyang ye nas rnam dag cing // rang snang ye shes dbyings dang de bzhin nyid las gud na yod ma yin// de phyir thugs
19a1(rgyud 'grel): chen pos 'brel pa'i 'gro drug dus gnas mus gsel snang // des na 'bras bu rang snang dkyil 'khor nyid du chos kun 'byung bar nges// don dam dkyil 'khor nyid ni stang dpal gnyis bsam bcu// gsal byas dang pas zhugs nas
19a2(rgyud 'grel): dngos grub yid 'ong mnyam par 'gyur// me tog dor te skal mnyam ye shes gang gnyer ba// gang gnyer ya mtshan dngos grub 'byung bar nges// bca' lngar mi ldan dang med dam tshig nyams na brlag par 'gyur te// mi 'grub gags su 'gyur ces rgyal bas
19a3(rgyud 'grel): gsung // rdo rje dam tshig bkod pa'i le'u ste dgu pa'o// / de nas dges chen rgyal pos sbyin la snyoms zhugs te// dbang mchog sbyin pa 'di nyid 'gro ba'i mched du brjod// spyi dang khyad par ma thob pa skyon dang rdzas dang 'bras bu lnga'o// sbyin
19a4(rgyud 'grel): yab yum phyag rgyar bsgom te sbyor ba las// bde mchog yig 'bru tshegs su rdo rje'i lam nas mkha' la 'khyil// rdo rje rtse nas gan du snyims zhing so so'i dkyil 'khor bsgyur// so so nyan dang bsgrub dang las 'chang slob dpon nyid dang lnga'o// nyan pa sna bar
19a5(rgyud 'grel): sems spros gzhal yas gang na dang bcas// traM gnyis las ni rin chen phyag rgya bskur gyur gsal spro thims// gsang gsum gnyen cha mi smra tshig bshang bsgrags// bsgrib pa snying khar de bzhin sgyu 'phrul dkyil 'khor nyid// rdo rje gzungs dang mchod dang
19a6(rgyud 'grel): sbyor dang tshig bshang bsgrags// las ni lag par de bzhin las rigs spyi stim bya// las dang po 'byung bar bka' yis rab tu bsgrags// 'chang ba lce la bad+ma'i rigs yin te// snod mthun gsang ba grags pa'i tshig bshang brjod// slob dpon yan lag lnga
19b1(rgyud 'grel): la ni khro'i tshem bu lngas// dkyil 'khor byed dang dbang sbyin ces par bka' yis bsgrags// skyon ni bla ma ma mnyes lnga po mthob bar// lnga por rlom pa dngos grub med brlag nges// de dus rdzas kyi rnam pa dgos pa yang // chos kyi rgyal tshab thob phyir
19b2(rgyud 'grel): rigs lnga'i dbu brgyan sbyin// shes byo ma dmongs sna tshogs dar gyi gcod pan te// gzungs dang ting 'dzin me tog 'dreng ba btags// gzhan gyis mi thub brgya gram go cha bskon// bdud las rgyal ba'i chu srin rgyal mtshan btang// mi d+ha mi
19b3(rgyud 'grel): shig rigs kyi phyag rgyas btab// tshe gdungs bsel phyir skyob pa gdugs kyi dgab// bag chags sbyangs phyir yum lnga'i bum pa bstan// 'dod pa'i yon tan longs spyod bza' btung btab// nges pa'i 'bras bu smin phyir snying po lnga// 'di dag
19b4(rgyud 'grel): rjerdzas su sbyin ces rgyal bas gsung // 'bras bu rgyal sras ngan song med pa dang // 'jig rten tshe dang bde ba thob pa dang // mtho rigs lnga mi thar pa'i chos kyi rgyal por 'gyuraro// dbang sbyin pa'i le'u ste bcu pa'o//
19b5(rgyud 'grel): sa bcom ldan 'das dgyes pa chen pos// rgyal po'i tshigs su dbang bskur mnyam bzhag te// bde ba'i mchog gi le'u 'di 'gro ba'i mched du brjod// rnal 'byor dgongs pa'i khyad par dang // byin rlabs pa dang sbyor sgrol dang // 'jug pa 'bras
19b6(rgyud 'grel): bur bcas pa dang // 'i khro tshom bu'i drangs bstan pa// rnam pa drug gis yang dag bshad// dgongs pa rgyu gcig yig 'bru byin rlabs mngon sum rtogs rnams bzhi// rgyu gcig don dam kun rdzob dbyer mong ba// ma skyes sgyu ma snang dang rang bzhin
20a1(rgyud 'grel): med par gcig/ a o IM ste sku gsungs thugs rang bzhin// ma skyes sgyu ma dbyer med yig 'bru'i tshul// ras dkar dmar po mtshon gyi bsgyur tshul du// rgyu gcig yig 'brus chos kun byin gyis rlobs// lung dang man
20a2(rgyud 'grel): mi brten mi 'gal bar// rang rig blo yis mngon sum rtogs zhes bshad// rtogs gzhis chos kun mngon rdzogs rgyal po che/ \u0f7fgang zhig de rtogs tshogs kyi bdag por gsung // rdzogs chen rdzogs pa'i rnal 'byor zhes kyang de la ba// ji ltar yan
20a3(rgyud 'grel): lag lnga dang dbang po lnga// rnam shes lngas bsdus rnams smin oM du bsgoms// zhi khro rgyal ba yab yum byin gyis brlabs// 'dod yon lnga sogs yul gyi rnam pa kun// rnam pa ma yin yi ge mu du bsgom// zhi khro dbyings phyug yum du bsgom par bya//
20a4(rgyud 'grel): gos brgyan bza' btung glu tshig bro gar sprin tshogs kun// byang chub sems tshegs yi ge hUM du rab bsgoms te// spyang dang dngos grub 'byung ba'i dkyil 'khor mnyes// oM mu hUM nyid sku gsung thugs yin byin rlabs pa// sbyor ba'i gzungs ma lha
20a5(rgyud 'grel): glu'i bu mo 'am rigs ngan sogs// ni rgyas dag la dbye ba 'am dbade drag dag la mi dbye bar// mnyen bsgrub rnams bzhi rim pa rab tu tsam// bsnyen pa don dam byang chub sems shes yin// nye ba'i snyen pa bdag nyid pog rgyar bsgom// bsgrub pa yum
20a6(rgyud 'grel): nyi ba rdungs su byin rlabs bya// bsla chen yab yum gnyis med byin rlabs la// mkha' las sems 'dres bdag mcher rgyal ba mnyes// 'gro tshams nyi zla rdo rje ldi yis dngos zos na// nam mkhar 'gro dang mdog mngangs tshe ring ba// bran mo
20b1(rgyud 'grel): mchog gi bsgrub pa yin bzhin bdag por 'gyur// bsgral ba'i zhing 'gyur rgyu mchog rnam lnga po// a 'bras rgun 'brum pa na se dang ge rgyas a ga ru// mchog phran gzhan yang mchog gi bsdus pa kun// blo ngan 'jig rten zhesu bdo gshegs gsung //
20b2(rgyud 'grel): mkhas pas a ma las ni nyi zla'i steng du bzhag/ gtsug du ye shes sems dpa' ngan song sbyongs// che ba'i nga rgyal bskyed cing sor mo 'bru bcu bsgom// 'bru bcu'i 'od kyis rnam shes bsregs nas hUM du dag/ hUM nying mkha' la thims par 'phangs te/
20b3(rgyud 'grel): phyag rgyar bsgyur// de las sku gsal 'od 'phros brgyan dang ldan// gnyis su med par bsgrol zhes de la bya// don ngom skye med kun rdzob mig g.yor tshul// sbyor bsgrol bas kyang rdul tsam bya mi dmigs// 'jug pa 'bras bcas dag mnyam gsum
20b4(rgyud 'grel): dodang ba ni/ snang ni 'byung lnga gzhal yas yum du dag/ phung po bcud rnams rgyal ba yab du dag/ tshogs brgyud sems rgyud ye shes lhur dag rtogs// de che don dam ma skyes dbyings su mnyam// kun rdzob sgyu ma phyag rgya chen por mnyam// shes rab
20b5(rgyud 'grel): lha ngang yul rnams lA mar mnyam// des na thams cad dkyil 'khor kun du bzang po'i zhing // byed spyod nyid kyang tshogs gnyis rdzogs par rol// de phyir rang bzhin lhun grub tshogs zhes gsungs// bkra drangs tshe gas ngo dkyil 'khor byed pa'i tshe// yan
20b6(rgyud 'grel): lag rtse lnga po ma nyams yo byad rnams lngar ldan// cho ga lnga rdzogs tshogs 'dus dkyil 'khor gyis// nges par legs pa'i dngos grub dgongs pa 'grub// chom bu'i grangs kyang lnga dang gsum dang gcig/ rigs lnga rigs gsum rigs gcig tshom bu
21a1(rgyud 'grel): la// khro bo khro mo nyi shu'i 'khor lo bskor// tshem bu de kun gtso gzungs zung du 'khril// khro bo'i tshim bu grangs kyang de bzhin te// po nya phyag brnyan bka' nyan ci bgyi rnams// 'khor bar dngos grub las rnams rdzogs par byed// tshogs
21a2(rgyud 'grel): kyi le'u ste bcu gcig pa'o// de nas rgyal po dgyes chen pos// rol mo sprin 'phro brgyan bkod rnams bzhugs te// tshogs bsgrub le'u 'di 'gro ba'i mched du brjod// longs spyod sa sor 'grub pa'i khyad par dang // rigs 'dzin
21a3(rgyud 'grel): spyi dang rigs kyi rnal 'byor dang // 'bras bu'i khang par gegs meng khyad lnga'o// so so'i sgyu 'phrul bstan pa'i ting 'dzin gyis// phyag rgya lnga'i dngos grub rnam pa lnga// lhun gyis grub par bde gshegs rgyal bas gsung // rig 'dzin shes 'jug 'bras bu
21a4(rgyud 'grel): khyad par bsam yas pa// rtogs gzhi tshul rig shes pa'i mtshan nyid yin// yang dang ying du gom pa 'jug pa ste// goms 'thus sngon du gyur pa 'bras bu'i mtshan nyid yin// rgyu rkyen 'bras bu nus 'thur gang gyur pa// rig 'dzin zhes su rgyal ba'i zhing du
21a5(rgyud 'grel): grags// 'dod khams lha mi tshangs pa'i skyes gnas su// skye gzhi rnam par dag pa 'dzin mod kyi// rtog pa'i khyad par sa la gnas 'gyur yin// byang chub sa bcu bde gshegs sa gsum ste// de nyid dus ni pha rol phyin bcu byang chub pa'i rgyu// sbyin sogs
21a6(rgyud 'grel): rag dga' la sogs lhun gyis grub// babs kyi kun du 'ong yin shes rab pad+ma can// thabs dang shes ma chog 'khor lo'i tshogs chen to// rgyu 'bras rims don me yin lhun gyis grub// khyad par sa zhes lhun grub nyid la brjod// rigs kyi rnal 'byor rdza
21b1(rgyud 'grel): rje sems dpa' nyid// steng dbul mkha' dbyings nyi zla'i steng bsgom nas// rgyal ba'i dkyil 'khor ma lus bsgom par 'gyur// de phyir rigs kyi rigs zhes brjod pa yin// phyogs dus kun nas sangs rgyas brtsal kyang mi rnyed te// rang rig sems nyid
21b2(rgyud 'grel): rdzogs sangs rgyas kyi dkyil 'khor yin// de phyir sems las ma rtogs sangs rgyas gzhan du ma 'tshal gcig/ rang sems rgyal ba'i dkyil 'khor kun du rab sbyor bas// de phyir dkyil 'khor thams cad 'grub par 'gyur zhes rgyal bas gsung //
21b3(rgyud 'grel): rang sems dkyil 'khor nyid du rtogs chung na// cho ga lhag chad skyon min gags med yin// de skad brjod tshes rol mos bde gshegs mnyes// tshogs bsgrub po le'u ste bcu gnyis pa'o// / de nas bde gshegs kun kyang
21b4(rgyud 'grel): cig du dgongs 'dus nas// lhun grub dam tshig snying po'i sprin la snyoms zhugs nas// mdor bsdus gsang ba 'di nyid 'gro ba'i mched du brjod// gsang ba'i spyi dang mdo dang rgyas dang mos pa'i yon tan dang // rnyed dka' lam gyur rtang dang skyon dang rnam
21b5(rgyud 'grel): pa brgyad// spyi ni ma rtogs 'phyal ba rgyangs pan dang // log par rtogs pa mur thug mu stegs dang // phyogs rtogs nyan thos rang rgyal rigs can dang // yang dag ma rtogs byang chub shes bya'i bsgrib// 'dul ba'i las ni bya ba gnyis ga rgyud//
21b6(rgyud 'grel): dgongs pa'i don sangs phyis thub pa'i rgyud// rang bzhin sku gsung thugs gsang rgyud rnams kun// bkri phyir rang bzhin gsang don rgas pa rnams// yi ge sgra btags tshogs 'brel ming tshogs la// rten pa'i tshig rnams kyis ni rab mtshon ste//
22a1(rgyud 'grel): dgongs pa'i dbang gis don gnyis gab cing sbas// kun gyi khongs na gnas pa'i don de gsang ba 'di las 'byin mdzad pa'i// theg pa kun la mkhas pa ston pa'i thugs la gnas// de phyir gsang ba'i snying po de kho na
22a2(rgyud 'grel): de nyid nges pa'i khongs nas phyung zhes ston pas gsungs// 'byung gnas bstan la phebs ces de nyid yin// sna tshogs don 'chang smra zhing ston ces de la bya// mdo don dkyil 'khor bcu gnyis bsdus bshad pa// dkyil 'khor de bzhin nyid ces bya bar
22a3(rgyud 'grel): bshad// de bzhin nyid ldan rang bzhin dkyil 'khor gyis// gzugs brnyan lhag pa'i gzugs brnyan dkyil 'khor la// ting 'dzin lhag pa'i ting 'dzin dkyil 'khor bsgom// tshogs chen bya ba dkyil 'khor nyid yin te// dkyil 'khor las byung
22a4(rgyud 'grel): thugs rjes 'dul bar bshad// thugs ni byang chub rnams gnyis dkyil 'khor yin// lhun gyis grub pa'i dkyil 'khor mchog du gsung // bcu gnyis nyid du rgyud kyi don rdzogs te// gsang ba'i man ngag ces kyang de phyir brjod// rgyas pa de bzhin
22a5(rgyud 'grel): nyid ni rtogs dka' gsang ba spros med thig le te// dkyil 'khor kun 'byung phyir ni dbyings ces gsungs// rang bzhin 'byung lnga dngos meng shes rab yum// chen po rags pa thabs te yab lnga yin// gnyis med sems las sprul pa'i lha tshogs ni//

22b1(rgyud 'grel): bshad// rnal 'byor bde ba'i tshogs mchog mi zang rol mo yis// ye shes dges pa'i lha la mchod 'bul tshogs zhes pa// zag med rang rig bsod nams rgyu nyid kyis// ye shes rang snang sgyu ma'i dkyil 'khor rol mo mtha' yas mchog/ de nyid ting nge 'dzin te
22b2(rgyud 'grel): pa'i ting 'dzin gsang ba'i thig le yum gyi dbyings// thig le de nyid sangs rgyas kun gyi dngos gzhi yin// bde gshegs sku sogs bdag gi zhal mthong ba// rig pas dbang bsgyur dngos grub dam pa gzugs brnyan rnams gnyis yin// lhun grub dkyil 'khor
22b3(rgyud 'grel): la gnas dkyil 'khor ma lus nyid// rdzogs pa'i dkyil 'khor nyid du ma lus lhun gyi grub// des na dkyil 'khor mi zad brgyan du ma lus de dag bdag gis thogs// thugs rje rdzogs pa'i dkyil 'khor mnyam sbyar las// snying rje chen po'i dkyil 'khor mi

24b3(rgyud 'grel): bas khro la thugs rjes 'phros pas dregs pa ngang gis zhi mdzad pa// thugs rje dpal chen rngams pa'i cha lugs 'dzin pa rnams// khro rgyal rngams pa'i sku gsung yon tan 'phrin las dmang po che// dus 'di nyid du rnal 'byor bdag la brtsal du gsol//

24b6(rgyud 'grel): bcom ldan 'das dgyes pas nyid kyi dkyil 'khor bstan pa'i phyir// 'gro ba'i ched du dkyil 'khor de nyid ched du brjod par mdzad// dbyibs brgyan dang gdan dang mdog dang cha lugs dang // chas dang gsung sgra phyag mtshan btsun mo nyid dang 'khor//
25a1(rgyud 'grel): rnam pa 'di bcus 'bar ba'i dkyil 'khor lhun gyis grub// dbyibs ni ye shes me 'bar ba'i 'khor lo rtsibs bzhi pa// mu khyud gru chang sgo bzhi par 'khyams gnyis kyis gru bzhir mdzes// gnas kyi brgyan mchog thong ba'i
25a2(rgyud 'grel): 'phreng ba tshar gsum dbang tshad sgrol// sbrul lnga rigs lnga mnga' mnyes dug lnga lhun gyis grub// nyi ma gsal bsreg rang bzhin mdzad par bshad// mi'i rang bzhin 'bar ba la ni 'phro ba mang po 'khrig/ gdan mchog 'dul dga' mi 'jigs khyu mchog
25a3(rgyud 'grel): dang / stobs mchog ma hA hes thig le blong yang gzigs// dpa' bstan za bad stag dang gtum tung ngom gyis sder mo yis// dbang phyug che dang dri za gnod sbyin srin po gshin rje so sor gzung // de phyir che ba'i che ba dbang phyug yang ches gnon ces//
25a4(rgyud 'grel): bshad/ sku mdog drag po'i kha dog lngar snang ba// nyi shu rtsa lnga drag po'i mdog yin no// tshul dgu ldan par 'jigs pa'i sku zhes bshad// cha lugs rnam thar dbu gsum pha rol byin drug phyag/ zhabs bzhi bskyod med mthar phyin lam zhes
25a5(rgyud 'grel): sha chas ni zhing dang glang chen ko rlon stag sogs sku la gsol// bong sbrul nyi mas dbu dang 'gur chu phyag zhabs bsred par brgyan// gsung sgra hUM phaT la sogs 'jigs par bsgrags// steng gi 'jig rten la sogs phyag mtshan mtshon char bsnam//
25a6(rgyud 'grel): cis 'dul thabs kyi rang rang lag cha ma nges sna tshogs bsnams// btsun mo'o tshogs ni cha lugs yab dang 'thun par 'khril// de ltar yab yum bcu po che ba brtsis 'gyur na// dbu ni sum cus rnam thar sum cu mtshon pa ste// rig lnga dbyings dang
25b1(rgyud 'grel): ye shes rnam thar sum cu yin// dgu bcu'i spyan gyis nyon mongs dgu bcu'i mtha' la gzigs// drug cu'i snyan gyis lta ba drug cu'i mtha' bas na sang // drug cu'i shangs nas drug cu'i 'dul ba sprul pa 'phro// drug cu'i ljags kyi lta ba drug cu'i dul
25b2(rgyud 'grel): thabs 'chad// drug cu'i gnas su drug cu'i skur ston pa// drug cu'i thugs kyi drug cu'i 'dul thabs mnga'// zhabs ni bzhi bcu lam yang bzhi bcu bsgrong meng bkrol// dbyings dang ye shes kyis ni stag chang mtha' bcom pas// lha gnas drug cu rtsa
25b3(rgyud 'grel): gnyis 'joms zhes mkhas pas bshang // spyir na bzhi brgya drug cu'i dgongs pa bsam mi khab// bsnams pa brgyan gyis tsho ba bshad pa yang // dbu brgyan dang ni 'gur chu gsum gsum ste// dpung brgyan dang ni phyag rngub drug drug yin// sku la
25b4(rgyud 'grel): g.yang gzhi ko rlon sham thabs rkyad bcings bzhi bzhis brgyan pa'o// zhabs rngubs bzhi yin mi ris brgyan pa ste// lnga gnyis dag la spyir na nyis brgya bdun cus brgyan// de dag mtshan ma'i gnyer gyis ci rigs bshad par bya// gnas yul sgo sbyangs
25b5(rgyud 'grel): blas dang bi mo'i tshogs// zhing gi stan dang rang rang lag char bcas// ci bgyi zhes te sa ga bzhugs chas nas gnas// de dag dbu tsog spyan gsum snyan shangs ljags dang ni// sku dang thugs dang zhabs ni gnyis gnyis te// re re la yang bcu drug
25b6(rgyud 'grel): cha dang ldan// bzhi bcu rtsa brgyang tshogs la rtsis 'gyur na// bdun brgya drug cu rtsa brgyad rdzogs par bshad// spyir na brgya phrag bcu gnyis dang no nyi shu rtsa bzhir bshad// dbu brgyan 'gur chu dag ni re re ste// dpung rgyan zhabs rngub phyag rngub gnyis gnyis
26a1(rgyud 'grel): yin// g.yang bzhi la sogs lnga po bco dang 'thun// nga ltar rtsis na drug brgya nya mu rtsa bzhi yin/ sbyor na ba rgyan gyi che ba brgyad rgya dang ni dgu bcu bzhi'o// de lngar stong phrag gnyis dang brgya dang bco brgyad kyis//
26a2(rgyud 'grel): gdul bya'i dgongs pa bsam yas lhun gyis grub// 'gro ba gcig la'ang de kun tshang bas na// 'jig rten drug gi phyogs bcu mtha' yas pa// 'bar ba'i dkyil 'khor yin ces rgyal bas de phyir gsung // de bas de phyir rtsis las 'das ces mkhas
26a3(rgyud 'grel): bas bshad// khro bo'i dkyil 'khor bstan pa'i le'u ste bcu bdun pa'o// / de nas ston pa mnyes pa'i mchod pa 'gro ba'i don du 'di brjod pa// sbyor dang sgrol dang bdud rtsi 'dod yon dang // 'bras bu dang ni the tshom gsal ba rnam
26a4(rgyud 'grel): drug yin// sgrol ba bdag gzhan gnyis su med pa ste// thog mar bdag nyid mnyam pa'i don rtogs dang // bstan par bsgom ste sbrul ces rgyal bas gsung // gzhan ni rtogs ldan gnyis med blo can gyis// ma gtogs sems can snying rjes bsgral ba'i
26a5(rgyud 'grel): phyir Ta bdag gzhan gnyis med du 'i su gcig par d+ma ba/ gni 'ad dri ldag sems mnyam sbyor gyis// bdag nyid bde myongs bde gshegs mchog sbyor yin// mnyam pa'i grub rdzas bdud rtsi rnam lnga po// bdag dang mnyam pa'i bde gshegs tshogs la 'bul// 'dod
26a6(rgyud 'grel): yon bza' ltung bgo dang longs spyod lnga// de nyid dkyil 'khor yin te dkyil 'khor tshogs la 'bul// 'bras bu rang sems bde gshegs yon tan te// lha klu mthu chen gzhan las ga la 'byung // de phyir sems nyid las su rung ba'i rnal 'byor pas//
26b1(rgyud 'grel): rang lus phyag rgyar gsal cing som nyi med gyur na// rgyal ba'i dkyil 'khor dngos grub 'bar ba 'grub// de skad brjod pas mchod pa thams cad kun du khyab// mchod sprin dam pa bstan pa'i le'u ste bco brgyad pa'o//
26b2(rgyud 'grel): rnams yod par bya ba'i phyir// dam tshig 'gro ba'i ched du brjod// phun sum tshogs dang rnam ngag dang ni mnyam nyid dang // rtsa dang yan lag nyams rkyen yon tan dang // grogs ngan spangs dang rang bzhin dbye ba dang // dgongs pa'i don dang grub
26b3(rgyud 'grel): dang yon tan rnams// rnam pa bcu gsum gyis ni yang dag bshad// phun sum tshogs pa bla med theg 'di la// nyon mongs spyad kyang 'bras bu tshogs 'gyur te// tshogs kun rdzogs pa tshul khrims phun sum tshogs// rnam dal bla med mchog gi
26b4(rgyud 'grel): dam tshig 'dir// 'dul dbang sdom pa ji snyed gsung pa yang // 'dir 'dus pa'i de bsrungs dang du rnam par dag/ mnyam nyid zhes pa bzhi po ma grub te// don dam yod med pa mar mi dmigs shing // kun rdzob snang ba sgyu ma mig yor tshul yin pas//
26b5(rgyud 'grel): srog dang srog gcod bcad pa ga la yod// srog dang skyes bur brtags pa'ang log par brtags// bden gnyis dbyer med dbyings su ro gcig pas// thams cad rang las sprul te longs spyod ste// de bas rdzas dang ma byin len dang blang mi dmigs//
26b6(rgyud 'grel): chos kun sgyu ma ming tshig btags kun brdzun// brdzun la brdzun spyong brdzun btags ga la yod// chags med dbyings la rig pas chags pa dang // chags spyod nyid na chags dang chags med chags yul med// mtshangs spyod nyid tshang mchog tshang chen
27a1(rgyud 'grel): yin// de bas byed spyod thams cad tshogs chen rdzogs par rol// rtsa ba rnam lnga bsgrub dang gsungs pa'i dam tshig yin// yan lag bcu ni ye nas ngag mnyam rtog pas spang // rtsa ba lnga nyams sangs rgyas rigs med ston// 'dir yang bsgrub
27a2(rgyud 'grel): pa log 'gyur phyi mar yid du mi 'ong 'gyur// yan lag brda dka' 'bras bu med de ngan song ltung // ma nyams yon tan sangs rgyas mnyam thob 'gyur// grogs ngan rtsa ba'i dam tshig nyams pa'i 'chal ba dag/ nyams na myur du gso' la mi brtson pa'i gang zag dang //
27a3(rgyud 'grel): skad cig smras pa tsam gyis nyes pa brjod mi lang // rang gzhan rdo rje sangs rgyas bdag nyid yin// dbye ba rtsa ba'i dam tshig lnga po gcig la yang // rang gi mtshan nyid thabs dang rang bzhin med pa shes rab gnyis ces bya// gcig la'ang rigs de la sku gsung
27a4(rgyud 'grel): yon tan 'phrin las thugs// gzhi dang yan lag de ltar bcu phrag gsum zhes bya// de'i steng du gzhi mo yum bcu snun nas brgya drug cu// yan lag bcu po cig la'ang ni rigs lnga ste// de las sku gsung thugs te nyi shur 'gyur// de ltar spyir na gsum brgya drug cur
27a5(rgyud 'grel): 'a'agyur// dgongs pas 'gro ba'i rnam rtog ji snyed pa// de 'dul snyen por dam tshig de nyid 'phro// kun bzang chen po yon tan ji snyed pa// bsam yas dam tshig 'dis ni 'grub par gsungs// yon tan dam tshig bsrangs pa'i rigs 'dzin ste// srid gsum brtso dang
27a6(rgyud 'grel): dodo'o 'khor gyis bkur// sangs rgyas sras mchog dpa' bos spun du dgongs// bde gshegs thun mong min pa'i yul du zhugs// kun bzang 'jigs med phyag rgya chen por sbyar// bde gshegs spyod dang 'dul thabs bsam yas pa// de dag kun kyang rnam dag lhun
27b1(rgyud 'grel): gyis grub// dam tshig nyams kyang gso' ru rungs zhes bde gshegs gsung // gzhan yang bsam yas yon tan brjod mi lang // de skad brjod pas sangs rgyas nyid du 'gyur// dam tshig gi le'u ste bcu dgu pa'o// // de nas bcom ldan bde gshe
27b2(rgyud 'grel): dgyes chen pos// lhun grub byin gyis rlob par mnyam bzhag nas// rnam pa bzhi yis 'phrin las 'gro ba'i ched du brjod// thabs kyi bye brag dang ni khyad par 'phrin las dang // phyi nang gsang ba gnas kyi khyad par gsum// thabs kyis bye brag so so man+dal dang /
27b3(rgyud 'grel): lha'i khyad par dang ni ting 'dzin ngo // mchod sbyin dang ni rgyu dang gzugs pa dang // dgug dang gdab dang tshogs la dbul ba dang // phyag rgya dang ni dgongs pa gang yin pa// lhag ma byin ste rnam pa bcu gnyis yin// dkyil 'khor e baM ma ya tshegs mchog rnams
27b4(rgyud 'grel): gru gsum zla ga gru bzhi zlum por bshad// gtum chen rngams dang gzi brjid lhun chen dang // 'du 'phro gzi chen gsal ba'i gti rjid ni// drag dbang rgyas shing lha'i khyad par yin// khro bo chags dga' ba dang ni ting 'dzin dang // de dus 'phags pa mchod cing 'gro
27b5(rgyud 'grel): tshim pa/ ling ga'i rgyuni bdud rtsi lnga 'am zas lnga las// gang 'dod gzugs byas snying khar ming bris te// de'i rnam par shes pa dgug ste dbab// khro dang chags dang nga rgyal dga' 'phro dang // lhan ne gsal ba grub pa las bzhi'o// dbyibs dang kha dog
27b6(rgyud 'grel): mtshan ldan rab tu ga ba// de nyid so so tshogs la snyims par dbul// de ni lu gu rgyud du 'brel gdam bcings bskyod bya// dgongs pas sangs rgyas sku yang myos gegs tshig pa dang // dgub 'gyur phyir 'breng dbang du gyur pa dang // yid bzhin gter gyis na mkha'
28a1(rgyud 'grel): 'gengs pa dang // gtum chen rngams pa'ang mig yor ldan ner 'gyur// slas dang bi mo bran mo bran du bcas pa la// lhag ma byin te gang 'dod de la bsgo// khyad par 'phrin las khrag 'thung tshogs rnams kyis// bskyod pa'i bro dang phyag rgya'i
28a2(rgyud 'grel): gar dang ni// snyan pa'i glu blang sngags kyi tshig rnams kyis// ci 'dod la sogs las rnams 'grub par gsung // zhi rgyas dbang drag phyi nang gsang ba'i gnas// ljon shing can dang lcug khron rgyas pa'i tshal// shing gcig drung dang mes tshig phyi'i gnas// ma smras pa
28a3(rgyud 'grel): dang bu tra ma 'phel dang // skye rgyud med dang bkra mi shis gsang ba// ting 'dzin rnam pa bzhi ni nang gi yin// 'phrin las kyi le'u ste nyi shu pa'o// de nas bde gshegs nyid kyis dkyil 'khor che ba'i glu blangs pa// sku gsung thugs yon tan

28a5(rgyud 'grel): de de nas bcom ldan dges chen pos// gsang ba 'di nyid snang ba'i phyir// sdud pa kun tu bzang po la// bstan pa gzung bar tshad du brjod// kyai zhes su bos nas su/ gsang ba bsdu bar gtad pa mdzad// phyogs bcu dus bzhi'i bde gshegs ngo bo las//

28b1(rgyud 'grel): rgyal bas bshad// de kun nang na bde gshegs thams cad kyi// phyag rgya gsang chen snying po mchog du gsung // mchog 'di rtogs nas 'chad par byed pa'i skyes bu ni// rdo rje sems dpa' de nyid yin te gsang ba'i dbang yang rdzogs// ci'i phyir zhes na rgyal ba kun la

31b1(rgyud 'grel): bzhin gyi snang ba zhes kyang bsnyad de/ 'on kyang phan tshun las grol bar 'chad pas/ yul dang yul can du mi 'gyur te/ dper na rgya mtsho nyid rlabs lta bu'o// de yang shes rab dang gtan tshigs kyis byas pa ma yin pa'i phyir/ nges tshig 'grub pa'o//

31b3(rgyud 'grel): sum pa la gnyis kyi ngo ba dang rgyas pa'o// kyang gnyis pa la gnas pas/ spyi ngom ba'i ba ga'im la mngor bstan dang rgyas pa'o mthong ba nges par ma bas pas/ rnam pa med pa la yod par mthong ba ni/ me long ba/ ya' can lta bu ste/ rgyas pa la banyis kyi dang po 'khrul snang la gnyis kyi dang po ma nges pas 'byung ba

31b5(rgyud 'grel): ltar/ snang ba dang po rang rig pa// yul med gnyis phyir mthong med par// brtags pas tha dad gyur pa ste// de yang 'byung gnyis pa'ang bakhor ma nyams yang/ tshul bzhi gnyi khongs rdzas 'gyur// des na ma nges chad pa'i rigs// rang rgya phrul gi ngo bos dang po nyid//

32a1(rgyud 'grel): 'byor te de yang ngo bo dang mtshan nyid ril lhun gyis grub pa'i bdag nyid ni/ mtha' kun bral nyag cig ci yang ma spangs pa/ phyogs med phyogs kyi dngos gzhi pa/ ris can ris dang bral ba ni/ sgron ma nyid kyis kyang 'di zhes brtag pa
32a2(rgyud 'grel): mi zin pa ni/ sgro skur dang ngang gis bral bas skabs las nges pa'i lung zhes kyang bsnyad de/ 'di nyid las/ thams cad rang rig byang chub sems// de ni lung gi tshad mar bshad// tshad bzhi phab pa'i don yin te// zhe'o// rtul 'o na mun pa'i snang ba byung ba
